/></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell><fo:block font-size="24pt" text-align-last="center" color="white" background-color="black" display-align="center"><fo:retrieve-marker retrieve-boundary="page" retrieve-position="last-ending-within-page" retrieve-class-name="thumb0" /></fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:block-container><fo:block font-size="10pt" text-align="center" border-after-width="thin" border-after-style="solid">How to Develop Stylesheetfor XML to XSL-FO Transformation</fo:block></fo:static-content><fo:static-content flow-name="xsl-footnote-separator"><fo:block><fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-thickness="0.5pt" leader-length="33%" /></fo:block></fo:static-content><fo:static-content flow-name="Left-footer"><fo:block font-size="9pt" text-align="outside"><fo:inline font-size="17pt"><fo:page-number /> ｜ </fo:inline><fo:retrieve-marker retrieve-boundary="page-sequence" retrieve-position="first-starting-within-page" retrieve-class-name="section-title" /></fo:block></fo:static-content><fo:static-content flow-name="Right-footer"><fo:block font-size="9pt" text-align="outside"><fo:retrieve-marker retrieve-boundary="page-sequence" retrieve-position="first-starting-within-page" retrieve-class-name="section-title" /><fo:inline font-size="17pt"> ｜ <fo:page-number /></fo:inline></fo:block></fo:static-content><fo:static-content flow-name="Left-end" /><fo:static-content flow-name="Right-end" /><fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body" axf:kerning-mode="contextual" axf:punctuation-spacing="0%"><fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb1">1</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Preface</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="E2" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Preface</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL)<fo:basic-link internal-destination="a1"><fo:inline>(Source Information
 [1])</fo:inline></fo:basic-link> has been brought to the attention of a wide audience as a specification recommended by W3C on 15th October, 2001 for displaying and printing the XML document. The following is the general process to transform the XML document into XSL Formatting Objects (XSL-FO) and print it.
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Develop the stylesheet that conforms to the DTD of the source XML document to create the target output.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Input the XML document and the XSL stylesheet to the XSLT processor to create XSL-FO.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block> Get the target outputs such as paper-based output, PDF output, by the XSL-FO processor.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/XSL-FO_proc.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Generating XSL-FO and Display/Print by XSL Formatter</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The knowledge about XSLT and XSL is necessary to develop XSLT stylesheet. The knowledge about XSLT and XSL is necessary to develop XSLT stylesheet. As for XSLT, many reference books has been published other than the specification<fo:basic-link internal-destination="a2"><fo:inline>(Source Information
 [2])</fo:inline></fo:basic-link>.
Probably, XSLT is already much more familiar one, since it is often used for the conversion from XML to HTML.
The XSL specification <fo:basic-link internal-destination="a1"><fo:inline>(Source Information
 [1])</fo:inline></fo:basic-link>has a huge amount of contents, it has over 400 pages. It is pretty hard to understand this specification. But basically it is intended for implementers. It is not necessary for XSLT stylesheet designers to understand everything. You can fully write stylesheet by knowing some regular contents and patterns.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
This report explains how to edit stylesheet which is used for transforming XML documents into XSL-FO according to the example of <fo:inline id="EWB">SimpleDoc</fo:inline>. SimpleDoc is made for this report as a format to write a simple document. This is based on <fo:inline id="EYB">PureSmartDoc</fo:inline><fo:basic-link internal-destination="a4"><fo:inline>(Source Information
 [4])</fo:inline></fo:basic-link> presented by Tomoharu Asami.
To make it a simple, the number of the elements is reduced and the useful functions for writing and formatting documents are added.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">This report explains how to edit a stylesheet which is used for transforming a SimpleDoc document into XSL-FO. This report itself is the instance XML document of SimpleDoc.dtd, and it is then ready to be formatted by Antenna House <fo:inline id="E5B">XSL Formatter</fo:inline> with the stylesheet which transforms the SimpleDoc document explained here into XSL-FO.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb2">2</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Step for XSL-FO Transformation </fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EAC" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Step for XSL-FO Transformation </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Now, what steps are necessary to develop XSL stylesheet?  These steps are explained briefly as below.</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="fixed" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="30%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="70%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">Steps</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">Contents</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Know the structure of the XML document</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>First, the information about the structure of XML source documents is required. XSLT processor can transform XML document into XSL-FO without a DTD. But the information described in the DTD such as types of elements, contents of elements, appearing order of elements and values of properties are necessary for developing a stylesheet.

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Specify a printing form
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
This is the printing form as a final output, in other words the output specification. XSL is a formatting specification.  Printing forms has various range of specifications such as sizes and layouts of printing paper, layouts of head and body, deciding whether or not to output index, table of contents, and so on.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Apply a printing form to formatting objects</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>After determining the specification of printing, you have to know what XSL formatting objects and properties are applied in order to print in this style. It is better to practice how to specify by referring to a simple stylesheet. </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Develop an XSL stylesheet</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Put the instructions to the stylesheet in order to transform XML source documents into the target printing form. Map the XML source document to XSL formatting objects that can generate the output specification. The stylesheet have the similar aspect as the general programming languages, while it may be difficult if you do not understand the feature of the XSL.  <fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(1)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(1)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>Refer to the definition list template in this report. In XSL, Structure for control of the conditional branch can be made, but it is impossible to assign a value to a variable. The technique to realize by calling loops recursively is necessary.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote></fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb3">3</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">SimpleDoc Organization
</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EED" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>SimpleDoc Organization
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The following table shows the structure of SimpleDoc treated in this report. For more detail, refer to SimpleDoc.dtd.</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="17.5%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="22.5%" /><fo:table-column column-number="3" column-width="60%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block> Element</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block> Meaning</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Definition</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>title</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> title</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements)*
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>p<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> paragraph</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
(#PCDATA | a group of block elements | a group of inline elements)*

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>figure<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>figure</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(title?)<fo:block />
Specify a file by the src property.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>ul<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
unordered list

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(li*)<fo:block />
Specify a character for label of line by the type property.

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>ol<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

Specify format of number in the label by the type property.

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>table<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
entire table
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(title?, col*, thead?, tfoot?, tbody)<fo:block />
Specify whether to make auto layout or fixed by the layout property. Specify the width of the entire table by the width property.

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(tr*)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>tbody</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>table body
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(tr*)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>tr</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

table header
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements | a group of block elements)*<fo:block />
Specify the number of the columns to be expanded across, the number of the rows to be expanded vertically by the colspan and rowspan properties. The align property allows horizontal alignment to be set to left, right, or center. The valign property allows vertical alignment to be set to top, middle, bottom or baseline.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>td</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
table data
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements | a group of block elements)*<fo:block />

Specify the number of the columns to be expanded across, the number of the rows to be expanded vertically by the colspan and rowspan properties. The align property allows horizontal alignment to be set to left, right, or center. The valign property allows vertical alignment to be set to top, middle, bottom or baseline.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>program</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
program code
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | title)*</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>div</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>general block element
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
(title, (general block element | general inline element)*)
<fo:block />
The div element expands the type by the class property.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>a<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
anchor(link)
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements)*

<fo:block />Specify URL as the value of href property.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>note<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>note
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements)*</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>b<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
bold typeface
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements)*</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>i<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>em<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
emphasis
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements)*

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>code<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
program code of the in-line elements
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements)*</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>span<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
 general in-line element
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(#PCDATA | a group of inline elements)*</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>br</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
line break
<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>EMPTY</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The features of SimpleDoc are:</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
You can start writing a document from part, also start from section. It has a flexible structure so that it can map to various kinds of documents.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The number of the block element and in-line element are reduced to a minimum amount. The div in the block element and the span in the in-line element are defined to give various extensions.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The br element is defined so that you can break lines inside of the lists, or the cells in the table, also inside of the paragraph without ending the paragraph.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Output format of the list and table can be specified by the attributes.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The problem is that the content and style is mixed.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb4">4</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Hello! World</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EJDAC" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Hello! World</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EMDAC" axf:outline-level="2"> Simple Example of Transforming SimpleDoc into XSL-FO</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Now, we show the simplest simple stylesheet that transforms SimpleDoc to XSL-FO as follows.</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Source XML Document (Hello.xml)</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-16" ?&gt;
&lt;doc&gt;
  &lt;head&gt;
    &lt;title&gt;Simple&lt;/title&gt;
  &lt;/head&gt;
  &lt;body&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;Hello World!&lt;/p&gt;
    &lt;p&gt;This is the first&lt;b&gt;SimpleDoc&lt;/b&gt;&lt;/p&gt;
  &lt;/body&gt;
&lt;/doc&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">
XSL Stylesheet(Simple.xsl)</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-8" ?&gt;
&lt;xsl:stylesheet version="1.0" xmlns:fo="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Format"
                              xmlns:xsl="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Transform"&gt;
&lt;xsl:output method="xml" version="1.0" indent="yes"/&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="doc"&gt;
  &lt;fo:root xmlns:fo="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Format"&gt;
    &lt;fo:layout-master-set&gt;
      &lt;fo:simple-page-master page-height="297mm" page-width="210mm"
          margin="5mm 25mm 5mm 25mm" master-name="PageMaster"&gt;
        &lt;fo:region-body   margin="20mm 0mm 20mm 0mm"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:simple-page-master&gt;
    &lt;/fo:layout-master-set&gt;
    &lt;fo:page-sequence master-reference="PageMaster"&gt;
      &lt;fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body" &gt;
        &lt;fo:block&gt;
          &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="body"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/fo:flow&gt;
    &lt;/fo:page-sequence&gt;
  &lt;/fo:root&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="body"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="p"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="b"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline font-weight="bold"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;/xsl:stylesheet &gt;
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Generated XSL-FO</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;?xml version="1.0" encoding="UTF-16"?&gt;
&lt;fo:root xmlns:fo="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Format"&gt;
  &lt;fo:layout-master-set&gt;
    &lt;fo:simple-page-master page-height="297mm" page-width="210mm"
          margin="5mm 25mm 5mm 25mm" master-name="PageMaster"&gt;
      &lt;fo:region-body margin="20mm 0mm 20mm 0mm"/&gt;
    &lt;/fo:simple-page-master&gt;
  &lt;/fo:layout-master-set&gt;
  &lt;fo:page-sequence master-reference="PageMaster"&gt;
    &lt;fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;fo:block&gt;Hello World!&lt;/fo:block&gt;
        &lt;fo:block&gt;This is the first
          &lt;fo:inline font-weight="bold"&gt;SimpleDoc&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:flow&gt;
  &lt;/fo:page-sequence&gt;
&lt;/fo:root&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The above XSL-FO is formatted/displayed as follows.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"><fo:block border="solid" border-width="thin" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">
&lt;fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;Hello World!&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;This is the first &lt;fo:inline font-weight="bold"&gt;SimpleDoc&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E5DAC" axf:outline-level="2">Stylesheet Structure</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The above Simple.xsl and XSL-FO show the following facts:</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>A stylesheet is a set of templates. The descendant of the root element, xsl:stylesheet consists of xsl:template elements. Each xsl:template is applied so that the xxx tag of the source XML document may be processed by match="xxx".
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Formatting objects and the XML source text in each template are output to result XSL-FO tree. Then, templates that match to the descendant elements are called by an instruction of xsl:apply-templates. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">XSLT processor loads the source XML document, starts processing from the root node. It finds the templates that match each node, and processes them as described in the templates. The processor processes child elements recursively, continues until the processor returns to the root element and there are no more templates to be processed.</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EFEAC" axf:outline-level="2"><fo:inline id="EHEAC">Block Element</fo:inline>and <fo:inline id="EJEAC">Inline Element</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Please note how the XSL stylesheet maps block elements and inline elements in source element to formatting objects. </fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
In the stylesheet, <fo:inline id="EOEAC">p elements </fo:inline>are transformed into fo:block objects, <fo:inline id="EQEAC">b elements </fo:inline>are transformed into <fo:inline id="ESEAC">fo:inline objects</fo:inline>. The base of XSL-FO transformation is to map the elements of the source XML document to either fo:block elements or fo:inline elements according to the layout instruction.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The elements that intend to break lines by the end tag normally can be mapped to the fo:block objects. the elements of which the end tag do not intend to break lines can be mapped to the fo:inline objects. The attributes of source elements specify properties of formatting objects. In this case, the b element means emphasis and property of the inline object generated from b is specified as bold.  </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EVEAC" axf:outline-level="2">XSL-FO Tree Structure</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Next, please pay attention to the XSL-FO tree structure. The following illustrates the structure of the XML document.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/hellostruct_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Hello.xml Tree Structure</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In contrast, the tree structure of XSL-FO is as follows. The root of the XSL-FO tree is fo:root, which has two children, fo:layout-master-set and fo:page-sequence.  Fo:layout-master-set defines the page layouts and fo:page-sequence has a flow of contents arranged in in pages.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/hellofo_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">XSL-FO Tree after XSL Processing</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"><fo:inline id="ECFAC">fo:layout-master-set </fo:inline>that defines the page layouts should precede <fo:inline id="EEFAC">fo:page-sequence</fo:inline>（preceding-sibling）that is an actual content of pages. <fo:inline id="EGFAC">XSL processor </fo:inline>processes the XML source document from the <fo:inline id="EIFAC">root element</fo:inline>, seeking the <fo:inline id="EKFAC">templates </fo:inline>(xsl:template) to be matched. Therefore, <fo:inline font-weight="bold">fo:layout-master-set element should be an output from the template that processes the root element of the XML source document.
</fo:inline>
In this case, &lt;xsl:template match="doc"&gt; takes this processing.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The following node of the fo:flow is the same tree structure as the original document though the element names has changed.
<fo:inline font-weight="bold">The nodes existed in the original document</fo:inline> are transferred  as it used to be, using &lt;xsl:template match="xxx"&gt;...&lt;xsl:apply-templates;&gt; The result has the same tree structure.
In the Simple.xsl, the information described in &lt;head&gt;...&lt;/head&gt; of source XML document is not output. It is because the child element &lt;body&gt;is specified to be applied but &lt;head&gt; element is omitted according to the instruction of &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="body"/&gt;

</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb5">5</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Developing a Practical Stylesheet
</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="ESFAC" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Developing a Practical Stylesheet
</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EVFAC" axf:outline-level="2">Printing Form Specification</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">We can get only a simple output when an XML document is processed according to the sample in the previous chapter. In order to get more rich outputs, we add the following specification.</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always">【Page Format】</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="30%" /><fo:table-column column-width="70%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Item


</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>
Specification
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

Writing mode

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
lr-tb
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Organization
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
cover, table of contents, the text, and index are proceseed in order from the top.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Header, Hooter
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Specify the header, footer regions. Do not set text inside the whitespace on the both side of the body.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always">【Cover/Table of Contents】</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="30%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="70%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Item</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Specification</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Margin of paper</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Top: 25mm, Bottom: 25mm, Left: 25mm, Right: 25mm</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always">【Body Region

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>
Specification
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Margin
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

Consists of head, table, list, paragraph and image.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Writing mode
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>lr-tb</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Column</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>1</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Default font size
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>10pt</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Text align

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
justify
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Other conditions
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Place a header region and a footer region. The content of the footer region is fore-edge justified and changed by right and left pages. Place a borderline between a footnote region and a body region. The borderline is a solid, the length is one-third of the region body, left justified.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always">【
Header Region
】</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="30%" /><fo:table-column column-width="70%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>
Item
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Specification
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Extent
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>10mm</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Writing Mode
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>lr-tb</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Content
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Print the title
<fo:block />
Font size is 9pt. Center aligned in the inline progression direction, bottom aligned in the block progression direction. Create an index on the upper part of a page.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always">【
Footer Region
】</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="30%" /><fo:table-column column-width="70%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>
Item
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>
Specification
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Extent
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>10mm</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Writing Mode
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>lr-tb</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Contents
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Print a page number and a sub-title of the current page on the fore-edge side.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always">【Index】</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="30%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="70%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row
