font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Item</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Specification</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Margin</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Margin top: 25mm, bottom: 25mm, left: 25mm, right: 25mm</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Column</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>2</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Column rule</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>20mm</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EVLAC" axf:outline-level="2">XSL Stylesheet Organization</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">XSL Stylesheet consists of the following 5 files.
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="25%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="75%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>File Name</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Contents/Usage</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EMMAC">SD2FO-DOC.xsl</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Main body of the XSL Stylesheet</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EQMAC">attribute.xsl</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>The file which defines the property of XSL-FO collectively.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EUMAC">param.xsl</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>The file which defins values, such as paper size, as a parameter.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EYMAC">index.xsl</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>The file which defines the processing of creating an index collectively.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="E3MAC">article.xsl</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>The stylesheet for a document format without a cover, a table of contents and an index. </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
SD2FO-DOC.xsl consists of the following top level XSL elements.
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="25%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="75%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>XSL elements</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Contents/Usage</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="ETNAC">xsl:include</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EVNAC">Includes </fo:inline>the stylesheets divided according to the function.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EZNAC">xsl:param</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Specifies the value of paper size, etc. in the whole stylesheet as a parameter.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="E4NAC">xsl:attribute-set</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Groups and defines the property, such as block and inline, for every object of XSL-FO to output.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EBOAC">xsl:template match="xxx"</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

Defines the template for transformation described to every element of an XML document （"xxx"）. It is called by &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EFOAC">xsl:template name="yyy"</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
A subroutine of templates which is explicitly invoked by &lt;xsl:call-template name="yyy"/&gt;
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EJOAC">xsl:key</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Generates a key for an index. How to make an index is explained later in this document. </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">xsl:param and xsl:attribute-set are defined in param.xsl and attribute.xsl respectively, and are included in SD2FO-DOC.xsl.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
xsl:param and xsl:attribute-set are not necessarily required, but they have the following advantages:</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The stylesheet can be easy to see, easy to be handled by separating their roles. Properties of formatting objects are defined by xsl:attribute-set, while the transformation are defined by xsl:template.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>xsl:param provides a parameter at the time application calls the XSLT processor. It is possible to control a stylesheet processing externally depending upon the value of xsl:param. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">An example of using xsl:param</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- Specify whether to make a table of contents or not --&gt;
&lt;xsl:param name="toc-make" select="false()"/&gt;
&lt;!-- Specify a paper size --&gt;
&lt;!-- Refer to $paper-width, $paper-height for the value. --&gt;
&lt;xsl:param name="paper-width"&gt;8.5in&lt;/xsl:param&gt;
&lt;xsl:param name="paper-height"&gt;11in&lt;/xsl:param&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">An example of using xsl:attribute-set</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- Specify the property of formatting object that match to the p element --&gt;
&lt;!-- Refer to xsl:use-attribute-sets="p" --&gt;
&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="p"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-indent"&gt;1em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;0.6em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;0.6em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;justify&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-together.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">From here, the stylesheet is explained along with this SD2FO-DOC.xsl.
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb6">6</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Page Layout specification</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EXOAC" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline><fo:inline id="E1OAC">Page Layout specification</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The page layout of SD2FO-DOC.xsl has the following features:</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The page layout includes a cover, a table of contents, the text, and indexes.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block> The page layout for indexing a cover, a table of contents places neither a page number nor a document name. Therefore, it does not have header/footer regions.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The page layout for the text is different by right and left pages, and aligns the content of the footer region to the fore-edge side.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The top page of the body text is made as the 1st page.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Only the index page has two columns.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Therefore, 5 types of page layouts, a cover, a table of contents, the text (left), the text (right), and an index are required. The definition method of each page layout is described henceforth.
</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EHPAC" axf:outline-level="2">Page layout of Cover/Teble of contents</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Page layout of Cover/Teble of contents is shown as follows:</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/playout_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">The layout of Cover/Teble of contents</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The page layout is defined as <fo:inline id="EQPAC">page master</fo:inline>. Specifically, it's described as follows using the <fo:inline id="ESPAC">fo:simple-page-master</fo:inline> element.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Definition of the page layout in the stylesheet</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"> &lt;fo:simple-page-master  margin="25mm 25mm 25mm 25mm" master-name="PageMaster-Cover"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-height"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-height"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-width"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-width"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-body  margin="0mm 0mm 0mm 0mm"/&gt;
 &lt;/fo:simple-page-master&gt;

 &lt;fo:simple-page-master margin="25mm 25mm 25mm 25mm"  master-name="PageMaster-TOC"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-height"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-height"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-width"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-width"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-body  margin="0mm 0mm 0mm 0mm"/&gt;
 &lt;/fo:simple-page-master&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Although the specified value is the same, the page master is prepared for each considering the possibility of any changes.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Master name properties of fo:simple-page-master are set as follows:
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="20%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="25%" /><fo:table-column column-number="3" column-width="50%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>master-name</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Usage</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Refered Template </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
PageMaster-Cover</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>For a cover
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>&lt;xsl:template match="doc/head"&gt;</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
PageMaster-TOC</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>for a table of contents
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>&lt;xsl:template name="toc"&gt;</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The next figure shows the XSL-FO tree structure in the site of where to define these page masters and where to refer to.
<fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/layoutref_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">FO tree structure relating to page layout</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E5AAE" axf:outline-level="2">Body - <fo:inline id="EBBAE">Change Page Layout on Right and Left pages
</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In this document, the page layout changes by right and left page. In XSL-FO, the layout change on right and left page can be made by grouping the <fo:inline id="EEBAE">even-page layout</fo:inline> and <fo:inline id="EGBAE">odd-page layout</fo:inline>, then changing by turns.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Create two fo:simple-page-master, one for left pages and another for right pages, and groups them by <fo:inline id="EKBAE">fo:page-sequence-master</fo:inline>. <fo:inline id="EMBAE">fo:repeatable-page-master-alternatives</fo:inline> is used for repeating two page layouts by turns. The <fo:inline id="EOBAE">odd-or-even property</fo:inline> of <fo:inline id="EQBAE">fo:conditional-page-master-reference</fo:inline> is used to specify the conditions on which the selection of the alternative is made.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">It is described in the stylesheet as follows:</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">FO tree structure relating to page layout</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"> &lt;fo:simple-page-master margin="10mm 00mm 10mm 00mm" master-name="PageMaster-Left"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-height"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-height-default"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-width"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-width-default"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-body margin="15mm 25mm 15mm 25mm"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-before region-name="Left-header" extent="10mm" display-align="after"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-after region-name="Left-footer" extent="10mm" display-align="before"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-start region-name="Left-start" extent="20mm"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-end region-name="Left-end" extent="20mm"/&gt;
 &lt;/fo:simple-page-master&gt;

 &lt;fo:simple-page-master margin="10mm 00mm 10mm 00mm" master-name="PageMaster-Right"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-height"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-height-default"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-width"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-width-default"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-body margin="15mm 25mm 15mm 25mm"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-before region-name="Right-header" extent="10mm" display-align="after"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-after region-name="Right-footer" extent="10mm" display-align="before"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-start region-name="Right-start" extent="20mm"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-end region-name="Right-end" extent="20mm"/&gt;
 &lt;/fo:simple-page-master&gt;

 &lt;fo:page-sequence-master master-name="PageMaster"&gt;
  &lt;fo:repeatable-page-master-alternatives&gt;
   &lt;fo:conditional-page-master-reference master-reference="PageMaster-Left" odd-or-even="even"/&gt;
   &lt;fo:conditional-page-master-reference master-reference="PageMaster-Right" odd-or-even="odd"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:repeatable-page-master-alternatives&gt;
 &lt;/fo:page-sequence-master&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EWBAE" axf:outline-level="2">Index - <fo:inline id="EZBAE">Two-Column Layout</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The page layout of an index is two-column layout. In XSL-FO, the number of column is specified to the <fo:inline id="E3BAE">column-count </fo:inline> property  of fo:region-body.In other word, although column layout can be specified per page, the number of columns cannot be changed in the middle of a page. However, the block object can be arranged as span -all layout by the  <fo:inline id="E5BAE">span="all" </fo:inline> property. The column gap can be specified by the <fo:inline id="EACAE">colomn-gap</fo:inline> property belonging to fo:region-body. These page layouts are described in the following stylesheet.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Definition of page layouts in the stylesheet</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"> &lt;fo:simple-page-master margin="25mm 25mm 25mm 25mm" master-name="PageMaster-index"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-height"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-height-default"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="page-width"&gt;
   &lt;xsl:value-of select="$paper-width-default"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;fo:region-body margin="00mm 00mm 00mm 00mm" column-count="2" column-gap="20mm"/&gt;
 &lt;/fo:simple-page-master&gt;</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb7">7</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Output Control as a Whole</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EFCAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Output Control as a Whole</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>FO tree is generated in order of <fo:inline id="EPCAE">fo:page-sequence</fo:inline> of the front cover, fo:page-sequene of the table of contents, fo:page-sequence of the body of document. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The front cover and the table of contents cannot be created by the stylesheet made in order of the XML source document, so you have to make the subroutine templates that create the front cover and the table of contents.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>These processings are controlled by the templates that process the doc element, that is the root element.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The templates that process the doc elements created according to the requirement for processing conditions are shown below. As required they are creaged in order of fo:layout-master-set outputs, a front cover, a table of contents and the body text. It is possible for the attributes of doc elements to control whether to make these or not. It is possible to control whether to output a cover/a table of contents or not by specifying the properties of the doc element or the external parameters. For example, a cover is not outputted by specifying &lt;doc cover="false"&gt;. A table of contents is not outputted by specifying 'false' to the value of toc-make.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process the doc elements</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:param name="toc-make" select="false()"/&gt;
&lt;xsl:param name="cover-make" select="false()"/&gt;
&lt;xsl:template match="doc"&gt;
  &lt;fo:root xmlns:fo="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Format"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:call-template name="xml-lang"/&gt;
    &lt;fo:layout-master-set&gt;
    &lt;!-- Specify the page layout (fo:simple-page-master). This part is omitted. --&gt;
    &lt;/fo:layout-master-set&gt;
    &lt;!-- Make a front cover processed by the head elements. --&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="$cover-make or @cover!='false'"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="head"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;!-- Call the template that creates a table of contents. --&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="$toc-make or @toc!='false'"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:call-template name="toc"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;!-- Process the text (descendants of the body elements) --&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="body"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:root&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb8">8</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Cover</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EXCAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline><fo:inline id="E1CAE">Cover</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Output <fo:inline id="ECDAE">title</fo:inline>, <fo:inline id="EEDAE">date </fo:inline>and <fo:inline id="EGDAE">author </fo:inline>to a cover page. which are children of the <fo:inline id="EIDAE">head element </fo:inline>in the cover page. but not output the abstract.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The width of the block that contains the title is 130mm, the height is 30mm, and the block must be centered, using gray for the background color, dark gray for the border color. The title is placed 25mm down from the margin top, and make a 122mm height space between the title and the author to be written next. Use the font size 24pt, font style sans-serif. the text must be centered inside the block.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The width of the block that contains the date is 160mm and the block must be centered, using no background color, no border. Use the font size 14pt, font style serif. Make a 5mm height space between the date and the author.。</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The width of the block that contains the author is 160mm and the block must be centered, using no background color, no border. Use the font size 14pt, font style serif. When an image of logotype is specified to the author, place it preceding the author.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The cover is created by the templates that process the head. </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The layout specification of a title portion is arranged by the portion of name="cover.title" in xsl:attribute-set.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Layout specification of title, author, date.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- cover --&gt;
&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="cover.title" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;25mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before.conditionality"&gt;retain&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;122mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;24pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"sans-serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align-last"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="start-indent"&gt;18mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="width"&gt;130mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="height"&gt;30mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="background-color"&gt;#EEEEEE&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-style"&gt;outset&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-color"&gt;#888888&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-top"&gt;5pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-bottom"&gt;5pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="cover.date" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;5mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;14pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align-last"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="width"&gt;160mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="cover.author" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;14pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align-last"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="width"&gt;160mm&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Followings shows the point which should be aware of:
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>In order to layout the title, we use <fo:inline id="EWDAE">fo:block-container</fo:inline>.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The Property <fo:inline id="E1DAE">space-before</fo:inline> ="25 mm" is specified to the fo:block-container. This title becomes the first block of the region body. However, space-before in the first block of this region body will be discarded by default, and a title will be arranged at the upper end of this region body. By considering as <fo:inline id="E3DAE">space-before.conditionality</fo:inline>="retain", a space can be obtained compulsorily.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
If the logo attribute is specified to the author, it is rendered as the image. This is processed by the author.logo.img template. The pos attribute specify to put the image on the left or top of the author. The example of an author name with a picture may be shown at the cover of this document.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that transform the head elements</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="doc/head"&gt;
  &lt;fo:page-sequence master-reference="PageMaster-Cover"&gt;
    &lt;fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body"&gt;
     &lt;fo:block-container xsl:use-attribute-sets="cover.title"&gt;
       &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="/doc/head/title"/&gt;
     &lt;/fo:block-container&gt;
      &lt;fo:block-container xsl:use-attribute-sets="cover.date"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="/doc/head/date"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block-container&gt;
      &lt;fo:block-container xsl:use-attribute-sets="cover.author"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="/doc/head/author"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block-container&gt;
    &lt;/fo:flow&gt;
  &lt;/fo:page-sequence&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="doc/head/title"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block start-indent="0mm"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="doc/head/date"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="doc/head/author"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="@logo"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:call-template name="author.logo.img"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="author.logo.img"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="@pos='side'"&gt;
      &lt;fo:inline space-end="1em"&gt;
        &lt;fo:external-graphic src="{@logo}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:if test="@width and @height"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-width"&gt;
              &lt;xsl:value-of select="@width"/&gt;
            &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
            &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-height"&gt;
              &lt;xsl:value-of select="@height"/&gt;
            &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
        &lt;/fo:external-graphic&gt;
      &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
      &lt;fo:block space-after="1em"&gt;
        &lt;fo:external-graphic src="{@logo}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:if test="@width and @height"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-width"&gt;
              &lt;xsl:value-of select="@width"/&gt;
            &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
            &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-height"&gt;
              &lt;xsl:value-of select="@height"/&gt;
            &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
        &lt;/fo:external-graphic&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The template structure is very simple.
xsl:use-attribute-sets calls a group of properties defined by the xsl:attribute-set element and applies them to fo:block-container that matches to each title, date and author.
In each fo:block-container, each template is applied to each element of title, date, and author.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb9">9</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Table of Contents</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EEEAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline><fo:inline id="EHEAE">Table of Contents</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>A table of contents is positioned next to the cover by feeding a page. The title is "Table of Contents". The background color is gray.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>A table of contents is created by collecting the title elements of of part, chapter, section, subsection, and subsubsection in an XML document. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The contents of each line consist of the each title in the part, chapter, section, subsection, leaders (rows of dots) and a page number.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Space before, left indent, font size, font weight are specified in each line according to the nest level of each part, chapter, section, subsection.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The internal link from each line of a table of contents to the title in the text is set for a PDF output.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ESEAE" axf:outline-level="2">Templates for Creating a table of contents</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">A table of contents is created by the toc template. The toc template is called from the templates that process the root elements doc, by using &lt;xsl:call-template name="toc"&gt;</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Toc template</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template name="toc"&gt;
  &lt;!-- generate fo:page-sequence--&gt;
    &lt;fo:page-sequence master-reference="PageMaster-TOC"&gt;
    &lt;!-- generate flow applied to region-body --&gt;
    &lt;fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body" &gt;
      &lt;!--generate a block of table of contents--&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="div.toc"&gt;
        &lt;!--generate the title “Table of Contents”--&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h2"&gt;Table of Contents&lt;/fo:block&gt;
        &lt;!-- select the elements of part, chapter, section, subsection,
                 subsubsection from the whole XML documents--&gt;
        &lt;xsl:for-each select="//part |
                              //chapter |
                              //section |
                              //subsection |
                              //subsubsection"&gt;
          &lt;!-- apply template for each element
               to generate each line of the contents.--&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="toc.line"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:for-each&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:flow&gt;
  &lt;/fo:page-sequence&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The toc template processes a table of contents in the following order.
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Create a new page-sequence. This page-sequence refer to fo:simple-page-master described in master-reference="PageMaster-TOC" for a new page layout. Because the new page-sequence is created, the page is broken when it is printed.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Next, generate fo:flow object in the region-body. Create a block that contains a whole table of contents by applying attribute-set that is a name of div.toc. This attribute-set specifies the background color gray. Then, create a title "Table of Contents".</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>xsl:for-each select="..." is used to create a set of nodes consisting of parts, characters, sections, subsections, subsubsections of the whole document. Then, each node is sent to toc.line template that processes a line of the contents. Lines of a table of contents are alined in the order of appearance of the corresponded node in the XML document tree.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
This template is called from the template that processes the doc elements. So, "current node" is the doc element node. xsl:for-each change this <fo:inline id="E6EAE">current node </fo:inline>into each node group specified by the select attribute. Therefore, the current node is one of the five elements, part, chapter, section, subsection, and subsubsection in the toc.line template. When xsl:for-each finished processing, the current node returns to the previous doc element node.xsl:for-each</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EBFAE" axf:outline-level="2">Templates for Creating Lines of TOC</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The toc.line template creates a line of contents</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">toc.line templates that create each line of contents</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- global parameter and variable used when creating the table of contents. --&gt;
&lt;xsl:param name="toc-level-default" select="3"/&gt;
&lt;!-- The template that creates the table of contents --&gt;
&lt;xsl:variable name="toc-level-max"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="not (doc/@toclevel)"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="$toc-level-default"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="number(doc/@toclevel)"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
&lt;/xsl:variable&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="toc.line"&gt;
  &lt;!-- Count the nest level of current node,
    set the value to "level" local variable. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="level" select="count(ancestor-or-self::part |
                                          ancestor-or-self::chapter |
                                          ancestor-or-self::section |
                                          ancestor-or-self::subsection |
                                          ancestor-or-self::subsubsection )"/&gt;
  &lt;!-- Test if the nest level can be a target. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:if test="$level &amp;lt;= $toc-level-max"&gt;
    &lt;!-- Create fo:block for each line of toc. --&gt;
    &lt;fo:block  text-align-last="justify"&gt;
      &lt;!-- Widen the margin left in proportion to a nest level.--&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="margin-left"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="$level - 1"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:text&gt;em&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;

      &lt;!-- space-before becomes larger in proportion
           that the nest level becomes upper.--&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="$level=1"&gt;4pt&lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="$level=2"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="$level=3"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;1pt&lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;!-- font-size is processed in the same way--&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="$level=1"&gt;1em&lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;0.9em&lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;!-- font-weight is also processed in the same way --&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="800 - $level * 100"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;!-- Below is the data of the table of contents --&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
      &lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="dots"/&gt;
      &lt;!-- Output fo:page-number-citation.
           Formatter replaces it to the page number. --&gt;
      &lt;fo:page-number-citation ref-id="{generate-id()}"/&gt;
    &lt;/fo:block&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The toc template processes a table of contents in the following order.</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Count the depth of the nest of the current node (<fo:inline id="ELFAE">nest level</fo:inline>) from the root node, then set the value to a level variable.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block> If a nest level is on or below the level of "toc-level-max", it is processed. If not, it is not processed. The level of "toc-level-max" is specified by the <fo:inline id="EPFAE">toclevel property </fo:inline>of the doc element. If the level is not specified, the value is 3.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Create fo:block for each line in the table of the contents.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">4.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>According to the depth from the root node, determine the the property value of indent, font size, font weight.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">5.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Output title, leader, and page number which is the real data of a line in a table of contents. Enclose the title of a table of contents with fo:basic-link and set the link from the title to the body text. Generated PDF is set as an internal link. (Details about fo:basic-link are explained in the 'Functions for creating PDF' section in this document.)
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EUFAE" axf:outline-level="3">Counting the Nest Level</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The nest level can be counted as follows:
count(ancestor-or-self::part | ancestor-or-self::chapter | ancestor-or-self::section | ancestor-or-self::subsection | ancestor-or-self::subsubsection).
In other words, count itself which is a child of the doc elemnet or the ancestor nodes. This chart is shown below:
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/levelcal_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Count the nest level from the root element</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E2FAE" axf:outline-level="3">Setting properties according to the nest level</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Set fo:block properties according to the nest level of the current node. Note that in this case, the properties are not set according to the element such as part, chapter, section, subsection. By setting properties according to the nest levels, the table of contents can be generated without depending on the elements used, but using the same format. Next table shows the properties set in the stylesheet.
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="20%" /><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center" number-rows-spanned="2" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">
Property
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center" number-columns-spanned="5"><fo:block text-align="center">

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" text-align="center">5</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>font-size</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>1em</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>0.9em</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>0.9em</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>0.9em</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>font-weight</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>700</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>600</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>500</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>400</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>300</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EAIAE" axf:outline-level="3">Getting <fo:inline id="EDIAE">page numbers</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">You have to create page numbers that show the page where each part, chapter, section, subsection appear. <fo:inline font-weight="bold">Page numbers cannot be fixed until the Formatter finishes formatting the XSL-FO instance.</fo:inline>
In order to solve this problem, XSL-FO provides the function fo:page-number-citation. XSL Formatter replaces <fo:inline id="EIIAE">fo:page-number-citation</fo:inline> with the page number in the end of the processing. The <fo:inline id="EKIAE">ref-id property </fo:inline>specifies which page number is replaced. XSL Formatter finds the formatting object that has the same value in the id property as that specified by ref-id. Then, the page number that the formatting object belongs to is given. Therefore fo:block generated from the part, chapter, section, subsection elements must have the id properties. This mechanism is shown below.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/pcite_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Mechanism of fo:page-number-citation</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"> In the template, the <fo:inline id="ESIAE">generate-id()</fo:inline>function is used as the value of the ref-id property. XSLT processor generates the unique characters using generate-id() to distinguish the current node. </fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EUIAE" axf:outline-level="3"><fo:inline id="EWIAE">fo:leader</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Use fo:leader between the title of the contents and the page numbers. fo:leader is a special object for generating inline area. In the example, leader-pattern="dots" is specified. It plays the role to fill the space between the title and the page number.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">It is important that text-align-last="justify" in fo:block specifies to justify the entire line. So, the titles are left-justified and the page numbers are right-justified, then the <fo:inline id="E1IAE">leader </fo:inline>pattern fill the space between them.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
fo:leader property can specify various patterns as shown below. fo:leader properties are written in the left side.
</fo:block><fo:block border="solid" border-width="thin" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern=&amp;quot;dots&amp;quot;&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="dots"/&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern=&amp;quot;use-content&amp;quot; (content=&amp;quot;*&amp;quot;)&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="use-content"&gt;*&lt;/fo:leader&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern=&amp;quot;rule&amp;quot; rule-style=&amp;quot;dotted&amp;quot;&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-style="dotted"/&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern=&amp;quot;rule&amp;quot; rule-style=&amp;quot;dashed&amp;quot;&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-style="dashed"/&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern=&amp;quot;rule&amp;quot; rule-style=&amp;quot;solid&amp;quot;&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-style="solid"/&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern=&amp;quot;rule&amp;quot; rule-style=&amp;quot;double&amp;quot;&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-style="double"/&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern=&amp;quot;rule&amp;quot; rule-style=&amp;quot;groove&amp;quot;&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-style="groove"/&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;leader-pattern="rule" rule-style="ridge"&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-style="ridge"/&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The following pattern can also be specified.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="use-content"&gt;+&lt;/fo:leader&gt;</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block border="solid" border-width="thin" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">
&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="1em" space-before="3pt" font-size="0.9em"&gt;Arbitrary specification of a pattern
&lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="use-content"&gt;+&lt;/fo:leader&gt;
99
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EIJAE" axf:outline-level="3">Example of the generated contents
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Shown below is an example of toc created by taking the steps described.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Generated table of contents</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" margin-left="0em" space-before="5pt" font-size="1em" font-weight="700"&gt;
  Preface
  &lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="dots"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:page-number-citation ref-id="IDA4AIOB"/&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
See the table of contents in this report for an output example.
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb10">10</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Body </fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EPJAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Body </fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Process all the descendants or self of the body elements in the source XML document.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Each page layout of the body consists of a page header, a page footer, and a body region. The contents of a page header and a page footer are arranged in a symmetrical position by odd-numbered and even-numbered pages.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
When a page has a footnote, the line which divides body region with footnote region is drawn.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E1JAE" axf:outline-level="2">Templates for Processing a Body </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The body in the XML source document is contained to the descendants or self of the <fo:inline id="E5JAE">body element</fo:inline>. Shown below are the templates that process the body element.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process the body element</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- process of body element --&gt;
&lt;xsl:template match="body"&gt;
&lt;!-- start page number is 1 --&gt;
  &lt;fo:page-sequence master-reference="PageMaster" initial-page-number="1"&gt;
    &lt;!-- left page header --&gt;
    &lt;fo:static-content flow-name="Left-header"&gt;
          &lt;!-- snip--&gt;
    &lt;/fo:static-content&gt;
    &lt;!-- right page header --&gt;
    &lt;fo:static-content flow-name="Right-header"&gt;
          &lt;!-- snip--&gt;
    &lt;/fo:static-content&gt;
    &lt;!-- left page footer --&gt;
    &lt;fo:static-content flow-name="Left-footer"&gt;
          &lt;!-- snip --&gt;
    &lt;/fo:static-content&gt;
    &lt;!-- right page footer --&gt;
    &lt;fo:static-content flow-name="Right-footer"&gt;
          &lt;!-- snip --&gt;
    &lt;/fo:static-content&gt;

    &lt;!-- leader for footnote-separator --&gt;
    &lt;fo:static-content flow-name="xsl-footnote-separator"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="rule" rule-thickness="0.5pt" leader-length="33%"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:static-content&gt;

    &lt;!-- body --&gt;
    &lt;fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:flow&gt;
  &lt;/fo:page-sequence&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">This template pocesses the body elements as shown below.</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Generate a fo:page-sequence based on the new "PageMaster", the page layout right after the table of contents is changed.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Set header/footer regions based on the page layout. Place the title of the document in the header, page numbers in the footer.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Create a border region between the body and the footnote by using leaders.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">4.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Create flow objects in the body region.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">5.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
xsl:apply-templates processes the descendants or self of the body element.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
A page header and a page footer are described in fo:static-content.
