In the body page, in order to change the page layout on right and left pages, four fo:static-content should be prepared which are used for the right and left pages of the footer,  and  for the right and left pages of a header. Moreover, the border between the text and a footnote is created using also fo:static-content. </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Four of fo:static-content are mapped to the region of a page as follows. The layout for right and left pages are defined in fo:simple-page-master of the body, which is prepared by the "Body - Change Page Layout on Right and Left pages" section in this document, then the header region and footer regions of each page are named, respectively. On the other hand, <fo:inline id="ENKAE">flow-name </fo:inline> is specified to fo:static-content and the contents of <fo:inline id="EPKAE">fo:static-content </fo:inline> are poured into the region whose name maps to the<fo:inline id="ERKAE">region-name </fo:inline>.
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-header><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Page</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Name of region</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>Name of static-content</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Right page heade</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:region-before region-name="Right-header" </fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
fo:static-content flow-name="Right-header"</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Right page footer</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:region-after region-name="Right-footer" </fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
fo:static-content flow-name="Right-footer"</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Left page header</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:region-before region-name="Left-header" </fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
fo:static-content flow-name="Left-header"</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Left page footer</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:region-after region-name="Left-footer" </fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
fo:static-content flow-name="Left-footer"</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The border between a footnote and the text is created by fo:static-content with flow-name called xsl-footnote-separator. The fo:leader object is used for drawing a line. One third of the width of the body region is secured as a solid line.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The content of the body is outputted as a child of fo:flow.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EQLAE" axf:outline-level="2">Page Number Setting</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
It is possible to set up the initial value of a page number using the <fo:inline id="EULAE">initial-age-number property </fo:inline> belonging to fo:page-sequence. In SD2FO-DOC.xsl, initial-page-number="1" is set to fo:page-sequence of the body, 1 page is made to begin from the body in SD2FO-DOC.xsl.
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb11">11</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Page Footer / Page Header</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EWLAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline><fo:inline id="EZLAE">Page Footer</fo:inline> / <fo:inline id="E2LAE">Page Header</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Arrange a page number and a section title of the page in the page footer.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Output a document title in a page header. Furthermore, a thumb index with number is arranged according to the appearance of the top-level element among part, chapter, or section in a document.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EDMAE" axf:outline-level="2">Page Footer Output</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The contents of a page footer are outputted to fo:static-content. The contents are the same although the arrangement differs on a right and left page.
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Page number</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Section title of the page (Running footer)</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EJMAE" axf:outline-level="3"><fo:inline id="ELMAE">Page number </fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"><fo:inline id="ENMAE">fo:page-number </fo:inline> object is used for expressing a page number. fo:page-number object generates the special inline area, and XSL Formatter replaces it by the page number. In order to arrange a page number to a fore-edge side, text-align="outside" is specified to the propery of fo:block.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- Place a page number to a footer region --&gt;
  &lt;fo:block font-size="9pt" text-align="outside"&gt;
    &lt;fo:inline font-size="17pt"&gt;
      &lt;fo:page-number/&gt;
      &lt;xsl:text&gt; ｜ &lt;/xsl:text&gt;
    &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
  （Output a running footer (eplained later)）
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EQMAE" axf:outline-level="3">Running Footer </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The title of the section in a document is outputted to a page footer. Since the title of section changes for every paragraph, it serves as a running footer. For this reason, fo:marker and fo:retrieve-marker are used. <fo:inline id="EUMAE">fo:marker </fo:inline> is created to the title element in the text, and <fo:inline id="EWMAE">fo:retrieve-marker </fo:inline> is put on fo:static-content of a page footer. XSL Formatter replaces the portion of fo:retrieve-marker by the corresponding contents while formatting.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/marker.emf" content-width="70%" content-height="70%"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Specify the class name of fo:marker you want to replace with the retrieve-class-name property belonging to fo:retrieve-marker. retrieve-boundary specifies a range of appliance. retrieve-position specifies which fo:marker in the page should be sellected. (What appeared first or what appeared last, for example)
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- Set retrieve-marker to output a section name to the footer. --&gt;
&lt;fo:retrieve-marker retrieve-boundary="page-sequence" retrieve-position="first-starting-within-page" retrieve-class-name="section-title"/&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Generates fo:marker against the title element in the text. It is described as follows in the template which processes "part | chapter | section | subsection | subsubsection | appendix."
   </fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:if test="local-name() = 'section'"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:element name="fo:marker"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:attribute name="marker-class-name"&gt;section-title&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
    &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
&lt;/xsl:if&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Hereby, whenever a section appears in a document, fo:marker is generated as follows.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body"&gt;
  &lt;fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title"&gt;Preface&lt;/fo:marker&gt;
  &lt;!-- Contens of the section --&gt;
  ........................................
  ........................................
  ........................................
  ........................................
  &lt;fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title"&gt;Step for XSL-FO Transformation&lt;/fo:marker&gt;
  &lt;!-- Contens of the section --&gt;
  ........................................
  ........................................
  ........................................
  ........................................
  &lt;fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title"&gt;SimpleDoc Organization&lt;/fo:marker&gt;
  &lt;!-- Contens of the section --&gt;
  ........................................
  ........................................
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EDNAE" axf:outline-level="2">Page Header Output</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The contents of a page header are the following two.
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Title</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EJNAE">Thumb index</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EKNAE" axf:outline-level="3">Title </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The processing for outputting a title to a page header is only to output the title element to fo:block as follows.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;fo:block font-size="7pt" text-align="center" border-after-width="thin" border-after-style="solid"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:value-of select="/doc/head/title"/&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EONAE" axf:outline-level="3"><fo:inline id="EQNAE">Thumb index</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">It's also possible to output a thumb index to a page using fo:marker and fo:retrieve-marker like the section title of a page footer. In SD2FO-DOC.xsl stylesheet, 15 types of class names (thumb1, thumb2, ..., thumb14, and thumb0) are prepared and set to the objects which appear in a document (the top level object among part/chapter/section) in order. Each fo:retrieve-marker is set to fo:static-content which is a page header using a table cell. fo:retrieve-marker is not replaced if fo:marker which corresponds in a page does not exist. Thereby, the thumb index can be seen as moving according to the change of a section.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">A table model for creating the page header in the stylesheet is as follows:</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Creating a table for thumb indexes</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- a table with absolute-position --&gt;
&lt;fo:block-container absolute-position="fixed" top="0mm" left="20mm" height="15mm"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table&gt;
    &lt;fo:table-column column-width="12mm" number-columns-repeated="15"/&gt;
    &lt;fo:table-body&gt;
      &lt;fo:table-row&gt;
        &lt;fo:table-cell&gt;
          &lt;fo:block font-size="24pt" text-align-last="center" color="white" background-color="black" display-align="center"&gt;
            &lt;!-- It is replaced if a marker with the class of thumb1 exists. --&gt;
            &lt;fo:retrieve-marker xsl:use-attribute-sets="thumb-class"  retrieve-class-name="thumb1"/&gt;
          &lt;/fo:block&gt;
        &lt;/fo:table-cell&gt;
        &lt;!-- Create the rest 14 cells as well. (the last is retrieve-class-name="thumb0".) --&gt;
      &lt;/fo:table-row&gt;
    &lt;/fo:table-body&gt;
  &lt;/fo:table&gt;
&lt;/fo:block-container&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
In processing "part | chapter | section | --" in the text, the generation of fo:marker is shown as follows. The element name which changes a thumb index is set to Variable thumb ($thumb). Since it is the template which is common and processes two or more elements, you have to judge a current node. Using local-name(), the element name of a current node is investigated.</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Creating fo:marker for thumb indexes</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="part | chapter | section | subsection | subsubsection | appendix"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="(local-name() = 'part') and ($thumb = 'part')"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:element name="fo:marker"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:variable name="num"&gt;&lt;xsl:number format="1"/&gt;&lt;/xsl:variable&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="marker-class-name"&gt;thumb&lt;xsl:value-of select="$num mod 15"/&gt;&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:number format="1"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="(local-name() = 'chapter') and ($thumb = 'chapter')"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:element name="fo:marker"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:variable name="num"&gt;&lt;xsl:number format="1"/&gt;&lt;/xsl:variable&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="marker-class-name"&gt;thumb&lt;xsl:value-of select="$num mod 15"/&gt;&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:number format="1"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="(local-name() = 'section') and ($thumb = 'section')"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:element name="fo:marker"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:variable name="num"&gt;&lt;xsl:number format="1"/&gt;&lt;/xsl:variable&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="marker-class-name"&gt;thumb&lt;xsl:value-of select="$num mod 15"/&gt;&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:number format="1"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
    &lt;!-- Omit the rest. --&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">As for the class name (marker-class-name), 'thumb' is set asa fixed character sequence, then a number is given in order after that. In order to begin from 1 and to repeat per 15 pieces, the element obtains first what position it is as compared with the same element in a document using xsl:number. Next, the number given to the class name is realized by using the number of the remainder after deviding the position figure by 15.
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb12">12</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Head</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="E2NAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline><fo:inline id="E5NAE">Head</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Generate heads from the title of parts, chapters, sections, subsections and subsubsections.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The style of the head is not mapped for each element of part, chapter, section, subsection and subsubsection but mapped according to the nest level. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The head of the top level breaks page before the block.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Make it possible to set an image in the head.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EIOAE" axf:outline-level="2">Style Conditions of the <fo:inline id="ELOAE">Head</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Generally the style of the head is made according to the part, chapter, section, subsection and subsubsection elements, but in this case it is made according to the nest level. The conditions to be set are shown below. </fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-column column-width="70%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">
Nest level
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">attribute-set</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">
Style conditions
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">1</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">h1</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
font: size 24pt, sans-serif, Bold
<fo:block />space-after: 14pt, bottom border: solid 2pt,
<fo:block />break condition: break-before="page"
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">2</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">h2</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Font : size 16pt, sans-serif, bold
<fo:block />
space-before: 19pt, space-after: 5pt, keep-with-next. within-page: always
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">3</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">h3</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>font: size 13pt, sans-serif, bold
<fo:block />
space-before: 14pt, space-after: 5pt, keep-with-next. within-page: always
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">4</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">h4</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
font: size 12pt, sans-serif, bold<fo:block />
space-before: 5pt, space-after: 5pt, keep-with-next. within-page: always
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">5</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">h5</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
font: size 10pt, sans-serif, bold <fo:block />
space-before: 3pt, space-after: 3pt, keep-with-next. within-page: always</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
These conditions of style are defined in the following stylesheet.</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Style definition of the heads </fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- titles --&gt;
&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="h1" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;24pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"sans-serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;14pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="break-before"&gt;page&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-after-style"&gt;solid&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-after-width"&gt;2pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="h2" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;16pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"sans-serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;19pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;5pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-with-next.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="h3" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;13pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"sans-serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;14pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;5pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-with-next.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="h4" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;12pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"sans-serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;5pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;5pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-with-next.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="h5" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;10pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;"sans-serif"&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-with-next.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">keep-with-next.within-page="always" is specified to heads in order to avoid breaking pages before the next block. It is not specified in h1, instead, break-before="page" is specified. So the page break is inserted before h1 block, it is kept at the top of the following page and is kept with the next block naturally.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E6QAE" axf:outline-level="2">Templates for Processing Heads</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Templates that process the heads are shown below.  Heads are processed in one template intensively because the styles are selected according to the nest level.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process heads</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="part |
                     chapter |
                     section |
                     subsection |
                     subsubsection"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out"/&gt;
  &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="part/title |
                     chapter/title |
                     section/title |
                     subsection/title |
                     subsubsection/title"&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="title.out"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="level" select="count(ancestor-or-self::part |
                                          ancestor-or-self::chapter |
                                          ancestor-or-self::section |
                                          ancestor-or-self::subsection |
                                          ancestor-or-self::subsubsection )"/&gt;
  &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="$level=1"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h1" id="{generate-id()}"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="$level=2"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h2" id="{generate-id()}"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="$level=3"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h3" id="{generate-id()}"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="$level=4"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h4" id="{generate-id()}"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="$level=5"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h5" id="{generate-id()}"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h5" id="{generate-id()}"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="title.out.sub"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:if test="@logo"&gt;
    &lt;fo:inline space-end="5pt"&gt;
      &lt;fo:external-graphic src="{@logo}"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:if test="@width and @height"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-width"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:value-of select="@width"/&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-height"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:value-of select="@height"/&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;/fo:external-graphic&gt;
    &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The stylesheet that processes heads consists of four templates. Actual title of the head is created form the title.out template. The title.out template processes heads in the following order:
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Count the nest level of the element under processing and store the value to the level local variable.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Select the style of the title from h1 to h5 according to the variable, apply it to fo:block of the title.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Create the id property by generate-id() function and apply it to fo:block of the title.<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(2)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(2)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>Heads are referred from fo:page-number-citation of lines in a table-of-contents.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote></fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">4.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Call the title.out.sub template that processes images.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">5.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Output the text specified by the title element to the title .
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="inherit" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Although the template which processes 2nd part/title - subsubsection/title is "empty processing" (nothing is outputted), this is an usual practice for not outputting a title doubly.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The title line is outputted by the title.out template as shown proeviously. However the title character sequence will be outputted again because the title element appears while xsl:apply-templates processes the part/title - subsubsection/title elements. However, if the template which matches part/title - subsubsection/title is prepared and the contents are empty, the output of an excessive title character sequence can be controlled.
</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ERRAE" axf:outline-level="3">Example of a Generated Title </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Shown below is an example of a generated title by taking previous steps. Note that the result of <fo:inline id="EVRAE">generate-id()</fo:inline>function is stored as the value of the <fo:inline id="EXRAE">id property</fo:inline>.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Generated titles</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;fo:block font-size="24pt"
          font-family="&amp;quot;sans-serif&amp;quot;"
          font-weight="bold"
          space-after="14pt"
          break-before="page"
          keep-with-next.within-page="always"
          border-after-style="solid"
          border-after-width="2pt"
          id="IDA4AIOB"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline space-end="5pt"&gt;
    &lt;fo:external-graphic src="XSLFormatter.bmp"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
  Preface
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb13">13</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Processing Inline Elements</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="E3RAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Processing <fo:inline id="EASAE">Inline Elements</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The elements of <fo:inline id="EISAE">b</fo:inline>(bold), <fo:inline id="EKSAE">i</fo:inline>(italic), <fo:inline id="EMSAE">em</fo:inline>(emphasis), <fo:inline id="EOSAE">code</fo:inline>(inline program code) are transformed into the fo:inline objects which specify the character properties. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The <fo:inline id="ESSAE">a</fo:inline>(<fo:inline id="EUSAE">anchor</fo:inline>) element only output the referenced text first, output the contents of a target end of a hypertext <fo:inline id="EWSAE">link </fo:inline>of the href property. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>A <fo:inline id="E1SAE">note(</fo:inline>note) is transformed into a <fo:inline id="E3SAE">footnote</fo:inline>. A <fo:inline id="E5SAE">footnote citation </fo:inline>is usually (n). A sequence of numbers is applied to (n).
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The <fo:inline id="ECTAE">br</fo:inline>(break) element breaks lines.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The <fo:inline id="EGTAE">span</fo:inline> element (general inline element) only creates fo:inline.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EITAE" axf:outline-level="2">Templates that Process b, i, em, code Elements</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">It is very easy to transform b(bold), i(italic), em(emphasis), code(inline program code) into formatting objects. The templates create fo:inline template and set attributes to be applied. Bold is set as font-weight="bold", italic is font-style="italic", em also maps to bold. The way is different from the b but it becomes the same result. Code sets monospace to font-family property.  </fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process b, i, em, code</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="b"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline font-weight="bold"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="i"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline font-style="italic"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="em"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline xsl:use-attribute-sets="em"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="code"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline font-family="monospace"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
As fo:inline is applied, the line is not considered to break at the last of text. The example is shown below.
</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The inline element i becomes [
<fo:inline font-style="italic">italic</fo:inline>].</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The inline element b becomes [
<fo:inline font-weight="bold">
bold typeface
</fo:inline>].</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The inline element em also becomes [
<fo:inline font-weight="bold">
bold typeface
</fo:inline>].</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The inline element code (inline program code) becomes [
<fo:inline font-family="monospace">
monospace font (apply monospace font)
</fo:inline>].</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ECUAE" axf:outline-level="2"><fo:inline id="EEUAE">a (anchor) Element </fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The <fo:inline id="EHUAE">anchor (a)</fo:inline>element contains a Hypertext Reference property (href) which contains a <fo:inline id="EJUAE">URL</fo:inline>. It is a problem how to treat a URL. In this case put a URL in parentheses, output it after the text specified by the anchor element. But if the both contents are the same, the URL is not output.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process the (a) element</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="a"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="anchor-texts"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:value-of select="."/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;
  &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;xsl:if test="@href!=$anchor-texts"&gt;
    &lt;fo:inline&gt;
      &lt;xsl:text&gt;(&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="@href"/&gt;
      &lt;xsl:text&gt;)&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
    &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The example using this stylesheet is as follows:</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">'This example is shown on the Web&lt;a href="http://www.w3.org/"&gt; at the site of W3C&lt;/a&gt;'.
<fo:block />
 is shown as:<fo:block />
'This example is shown on the Web at the site of <fo:basic-link external-destination="http://www.w3.org/"><fo:inline text-decoration="underline" color="blue">W3C<fo:inline>(http://www.w3.org/)</fo:inline></fo:inline></fo:basic-link>
.'</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
'This example is shown on the Web site at &lt;a href="http://www.w3.org/"&gt;http://www.w3.org/&lt;/a&gt;.' <fo:block />is shown as:
<fo:block />
'This example is shown on the Web site at <fo:basic-link external-destination="http://www.w3.org/"><fo:inline text-decoration="underline" color="blue">http://www.w3.org/</fo:inline></fo:basic-link>
'</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">'This example is shown on the Web site at &lt;a href="http://www.w3.org/"&gt;http://&lt;em&gt;&lt;i&gt;www&lt;/i&gt;.&lt;i&gt;w3&lt;/i&gt;.&lt;i&gt;org&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/em&gt;/&lt;/a&gt;.'<fo:block /> is shown as:
<fo:block />
'This example is shown on the Web site at <fo:basic-link external-destination="http://www.w3.org/"><fo:inline text-decoration="underline" color="blue">http://<fo:inline font-weight="bold"><fo:inline font-style="italic">www</fo:inline>.<fo:inline font-style="italic">w3</fo:inline>.<fo:inline font-style="italic">org</fo:inline></fo:inline>/</fo:inline></fo:basic-link>.'</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Although the anchor was changed into the simple text here, in SD2FO-DOC.xsl, the<fo:inline id="EXVAE">link </fo:inline>of <fo:inline id="EZVAE">PDF</fo:inline> can be created by changing the anchor into fo:basic-link of XSL and formatted by XSL Formatter. Please refer to "Link Setting" of <fo:basic-link internal-destination="a-link"><fo:inline text-decoration="underline" color="blue">"Functions for creating PDF" </fo:inline></fo:basic-link> in this document for details.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E5VAE" axf:outline-level="2"><fo:inline id="EAWAE">note Element</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The <fo:inline id="EDWAE">note </fo:inline>element is transformed into <fo:inline id="EFWAE">fo:footnote </fo:inline>formatting object.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Template that processes note elements</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="note"&gt;
  &lt;fo:footnote&gt;
    &lt;fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:number level="any" count="//note" format="(1)"/&gt;
    &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
    &lt;fo:footnote-body&gt;
      &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="note"&gt;
        &lt;fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:number level="any" count="//note" format="(1)"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:footnote-body&gt;
  &lt;/fo:footnote&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">fo:footnote object in the XSL generates a footnote and a <fo:inline id="EMWAE">footnote </fo:inline>citation.the content model is (fo:inline, fo:footnote-body). The first child fo:inline expresses a footnote citation placed in the text. The next fo:footnote-body is the footnote text and it consists of the block objects like fo:block. Please remark that you should specify all indent values of fo:footnote-body to zero in order to cancel the inheritance of indent value from the ancestor of fo:footnote.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Shown below is a typical fo:footnote object.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/footnote_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Typical example of the note element and fo:footnote</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Generally, the same label as the footnote citation in the text is placed before the footnote text, and a footnote citation is usually a sequence of numbers. These characters must be generated in the stylesheet. Formatting object does not have the function to achieve these. The following shows the stylesheet processing.</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Output fo:footnote.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>

Generate fo:inline that includes a footnote citation by using xsl:number.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
A content of note element with the same footnote citation is put into a fo:block element that is a child of the fo:footnote-body.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
xsl:number is an XSL processing instruction.
<fo:inline font-family="sans-serif">&lt;xsl:number level="any" count="//note" format="(1)"/&gt;</fo:inline> searches all the descendant of the note elements under the root element in appearing order, finds out the same element as the current note element and formats the appearing number as described in "(1)",
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">baseline-shift="super" shifts the baseline to the default position for superscripts. Below shows the example of footnote.
</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"><fo:inline font-family="sans-serif">
"This is an example of footnote. Place a footnote here. &lt;note&gt; This is a footnote text. It is placed at the lower end of the body resion and separated from the text part.&lt;/note&gt;"
</fo:inline>
is expressed as:
<fo:block /><fo:inline font-family="sans-serif">
"This is an example of footnote. Place a footnote here.
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(3)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(3)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>This is a footnote text. It is placed at the lower end of the body resion and separated from the text part.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote>"</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ELXAE" axf:outline-level="2"><fo:inline id="ENXAE">br</fo:inline> Element</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The br element is an empty element, so it is replaced by an empty fo:block element. Then the line bleaks.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process the br element</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="br"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The following table shows the example of the process.</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">"In the paragraph, put &lt;b&gt; forcibly &lt;br/&gt; break a line &lt;/b&gt; because the paragraph is not finished, the property set before the line break can be used."
<fo:block />is expressed as:</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">"In the paragraph, put<fo:inline font-weight="bold">
forcibly
<fo:block />
break a line
</fo:inline>
because the paragraph is not finished, the property set before the line break can be used."
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ECYAE" axf:outline-level="2">
span Element
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The span attribute (general inline element) is only transformed into fo:inline. It can be extended
if any instructions are defined for the class attribute

</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">The template that processes the span element</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="span"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline &gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb14">14</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Processing Block Elements</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EIYAE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Processing <fo:inline id="EMYAE">Block Elements</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The processing of the block elements except tables and lists (ol,ul,dl) are explained in this chapter.  </fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Transform p(paragraph) into a block element.
Indent one character in the first line of the paragraph. Text align justify. Text align left at the last line. Spaces which size is font size x 0.6 are given before and after the paragraph. A paragraph is kept within a page.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Figures are placed by feeding a line at the appearing point, by centering. Apply the size of the figure if the size is specified. If there is a caption, place it under the figure.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Transform program element that contains program codes into fo:block formatting object. Apply monospace, use line feed, space as they are preformatted. The background color is gray. Output the caption in front of the program code.

</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Transform div(general block element) into fo:block.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EXYAE" axf:outline-level="2"><fo:inline id="EZYAE">p Element</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The p element (paragraph) is frequently used. The following shows the template processing the p element.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">The template processing the p element</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="p"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-indent"&gt;1em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;0.6em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;0.6em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;justify&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-together.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="p"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="p"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The templates are simple, and is only to transform into fo:block. The indent in the beginning of the line is specified by text-indent, the line justification is specified by text-align. And specify keep-together to keep a paragraph within one page.
</fo:block><fo:block break-before="page" /><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">This is the case that one line has the width of 21em.
</fo:block>
&lt;fo:block font-size="1.0em"&gt;
&lt;fo:block-container width="21em" padding="1em"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always" border="dashed" border-color="red" border-width="thin"&gt;This is the sample of a paragraph. The paragraph is transformed into fo:block. Specify that one character is indented by text-indent="1em". Specify that the content is to be expanded to both edges by text-align="justify". But the last sentence of the last paragraph is left justified. It's because the default value of text-indent-last is text-align="justify", it is justified automatically.
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:block-container&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
<fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"> In case that one line has the width of 25em.</fo:block>
&lt;fo:block font-size="1.0em"&gt;
&lt;fo:block-container width="25em" padding="1em"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always" border="dashed" border-color="red" border-width="thin"&gt;This is the sample of paragraph. The paragraph is transformed into fo:block. Specify that one character is indented by text-indent="1em". Specify that the content is to be expanded to both edges by text-align="justify". But the last sentence of the last paragraph is left justified. It's because the default value of text-indent-last is text-align="justify", it is justified automatically.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:block-container&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EJZAE" axf:outline-level="2"><fo:inline id="ELZAE">figure Element</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Figure elements are transformed into <fo:inline id="EOZAE">fo:external-graphic</fo:inline>. The following shows the templates that process figure elements.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process the figure elements</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="figure.title"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;sans-serif&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;10pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-with-previous.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="figure"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block text-align="center"&gt;
    &lt;fo:external-graphic src="{@src}"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:if test="@width and @height"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-width"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="@width"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
        &lt;xsl:attribute name="content-height"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="@height"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;/fo:external-graphic&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
  &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="figure.title"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">fo:external-graphic is generated and path of the figure is specified by the src property of the figure element. In case the size of the figure is specified by the width, height attributes, put them in <fo:inline id="EVZAE">content-width</fo:inline>, <fo:inline id="EXZAE">content-height</fo:inline>. Antenna House XSL Formatter can treat image file formats such as BMP, EMF, WMF, JPEG, TIFF, GIF, PNG, EPS, SVG, etc.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EZZAE" axf:outline-level="2"><fo:inline id="E2ZAE">program Element</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Program elements (Program code) are transformed into fo:block and display the fonts in monospace. The following shows the templates.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process the program elements</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="program"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="white-space"&gt;pre&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="wrap-option"&gt;wrap&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="background-color"&gt;gainsboro&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;monospace&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-size"&gt;9pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding"&gt;0.5em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="program.title"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;sans-serif&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;center&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-with-next.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;0.5em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;0.5em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="program"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="title"/&gt;
  &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="program"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="text()"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The program element and the p element has the common point that both generate fo:block in the template. But the difference is that the program element process only text(). There are no templates to process text nodes (match="program/text()"). So they are processed by the built-in template in XSL in order to process only the text node.
The following are important properties that apply to fo:block.</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Specify monospace in the font-family.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Specify white-space as pre. This has four meanings as follows.
<fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>linefeed-treatment="preserve" : Line feed character (#xA) is preserved. Do not treat as space, or ignore.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>space-treatment="preserve" : Characters classified as white space in XML except for #xA are preserved
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(4)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(4)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>White space in XML has space(#x20), tab(#x9), carriage return(#xD), linefeed(#xA). The treatment of #xA is specified by linefeed-treatment
