</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote>.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>white-space-collapse="false" : White spaces after processing by linefeed-treatment, space-treatment are not collapsed.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">4.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>wrap-option="no-wrap" : No line-wrapping will occur if the line overflows.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Specify the value of wrap-option as wrap to override the default value of space-treatment. The line wraps if the line overflows
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(5)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(5)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>wrap-option="wrap" is a default value. But it changes to wrap-option="no-wrap" by specifying white-space="pre".  This property overides wrap-option="no-wrap" by wrap-option ="wrap"</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote>.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
According to these specifications the text in the program element is formatted as pre-formatted text.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ES1AE" axf:outline-level="2">
div Element
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The div element(general block element) simply transforms into fo:block with no properties. The templates are shown below.

</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Template that processes the div element.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="div"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">You may change this template as you desire.
The example of applying the div element is as follows. This sample stores formatting object directly to the div element and output it.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Example</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="div.fo" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border"&gt;solid&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-width"&gt;thin&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding"&gt;1em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="div[@class = 'fo']"&gt;
  &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="div.fo"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:copy-of select="node()"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The template specifies to copy all the descendants of the div element directly to the output by &lt;xsl:copy-of select="node()"/&gt;. In order to use this function, you must specify following fo namespace to the doc element.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;doc xmlns:fo="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Format"&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Below shows how to use.
</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block>
&lt;div class="fo"&gt;&lt;fo:block&gt;This is the &lt;fo:inline font-weight="bold"&gt;example&lt;/fo:inline&gt; of embedding&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.5em" text-decoration="underline" font-style="italic" font-weight="bold"&gt;FO (Formatting Object).&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline background-color="#DDDDDD"&gt;You can format the styles as you like,&lt;/fo:inline&gt; free from the &lt;fo:inline font-size="1em"&gt;s&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.2em"&gt;t&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.4em"&gt;y&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.6em"&gt;l&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.8em"&gt;e&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.0em"&gt;s&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.2em"&gt;h&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.4em"&gt;e&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.6em"&gt;e&lt;/fo:inline&gt;&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.8em"&gt;t&lt;/fo:inline&gt;limitation. But it is very&lt;fo:inline font-size="3em" font-weight="bold" font-family="sans-serif"&gt;troublesome&lt;/fo:inline&gt;to write FO directly.&lt;/fo:block&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
It is shown as follows:
</fo:block><fo:block border="solid" border-width="thin" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">
&lt;fo:block&gt;This is the &lt;fo:inline font-weight="bold"&gt;example&lt;/fo:inline&gt; of embedding&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.5em" text-decoration="underline" font-style="italic" font-weight="bold"&gt;FO (Formatting Object).&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline background-color="#DDDDDD"&gt;You can format the styles as you like,&lt;/fo:inline&gt; free from the &lt;fo:inline font-size="1em"&gt;s&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.2em"&gt;t&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.4em"&gt;y&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.6em"&gt;l&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="1.8em"&gt;e&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.0em"&gt;s&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.2em"&gt;h&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.4em"&gt;e&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.6em"&gt;e&lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;fo:inline font-size="2.8em"&gt;t&lt;/fo:inline&gt;limitation. But it is very&lt;fo:inline font-size="3em" font-weight="bold" font-family="sans-serif"&gt;troublesome&lt;/fo:inline&gt;to write FO directly.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb0">15</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">
Processing Table Elements
</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EJ2AE" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>
Processing Table Elements
</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The descendants and self of a table element in the XML source document create a table formatting object.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The background color of the  head in the table is gray to discriminate from the contents in the table. And the line is solid, the line width is 1 pt.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Cells in the table store the cell data placing the padding, of which size is 0.3 x fontsize on the left, 0.2 x fontsize on the right, 2 point on the top and 2 point on the bottom.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
Process the properties related to the table format and make them reflected in the formatted result.
<fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
layout propery, width property and rowheight property of the table element.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
number, property. width property of the col element </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
height property of the tr element
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">4.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block><fo:inline id="E22AE">align property</fo:inline>, <fo:inline id="E42AE">valign property</fo:inline>, colspan property, rowspan property defined for th, td elements.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E62AE" axf:outline-level="2">
Comparing SimpleDoc Table with XSL Table
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In order to process the descendants of the table element and generate a table, it should be transformed into fo:table-and-caption formatting object. Let us compare the SimpleDoc table with XSL table. First of all, the SimpleDoc table is as follows:
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="17.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="22.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="60%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Element</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Meaning</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Definition</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>table<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> entire table</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(title?, col*, thead?, tfoot?, tbody)<fo:block />Specify whether the table layout is formatted automatically or it is fixed, in the layout property. The entire width is specified in the width property.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>col<fo:block /></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>column property</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>EMPTY<fo:block />
The column width is specified in the width property, the column number is specified in the number property.

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>thead</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>table header</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(tr*)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>tfoot</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> table footer</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(tr*)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>tbody</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>table body</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(tr*)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>tr</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> table row</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(th | td)*<fo:block />The height of the row is specified in the height property.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>th</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> table header cell</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
(a group of inline elements)*
<fo:block />
The number of the rows to be expanded across is specified in the colspan property, the number of the rows to be expanded down is specified in the rowspan. The align, valign propertys allows horizontal, vertical alignment to be set.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>td</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> table data cell</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Same as the definition of th
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
On the other hand, the object of the table of XSL-FO has the following composition.
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="17.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="22.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="60%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Element</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Meaning</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Definition</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-and-caption</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
entire table and caption
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(table-caption?, table)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-caption</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>caption of the table</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(%block;)<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(6)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(6)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>
%block; is defined to contain block, block-container, table-and-caption, table, list-block in the XSL Specification. Generally, it is fo:block, fo:block-container.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote></fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
entire table (except caption cells).
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(fo:table-column*, fo:table-header?, fo:table-footer?, fo:table-body+)<fo:block />
table-layout : Specify automatically table layout or fixed layout.<fo:block />table-omit-header-at-break : Specify whether to omit placing header or not when the page breaks.<fo:block />table-omit-footer-at-break : Specify whether to omit placing footer or not when the page breaks.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-column</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
table column
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>EMPTY<fo:block />
column-number : The number of columns
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(7)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(7)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>Use as a parameter of from-table-column() function.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote><fo:block />column-width : The width of the column<fo:block /><fo:inline id="E46AE">number-columns-repeated</fo:inline> : The number of columns specifying the repetition of the table-column. <fo:block /><fo:inline id="EBAAG">number-columns-spanned</fo:inline> : The number of columns spanned by table-cells.<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(8)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(8)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>Refer to from-table-column() function.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote></fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-header</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
table header
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(fo:table-row+ | fo:table-cell+)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-footer</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
table footer
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(fo:table-row+ | fo:table-cell+)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-body</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
table body
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(fo:table-row+ | fo:table-cell+)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-row</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>table row
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(fo:table-cell+)</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>fo:table-cell</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Table cell
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(%block;)+<fo:block />
number-columns-spanned : The number of columns spanned by table-cells.<fo:block />
number-rows-spanned : The number of rows to be spanned. </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/table-struct_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">
Table structure of SimpleDoc, XSL-FO</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Comparing these two, they have almost the same structure. Transforming into tables is basically considered to exchange the structure to another.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EDBAG" axf:outline-level="2">
Templates that process tables
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Templates that process tables are shown below.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Definition of the table properties</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="table.data" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="table-layout"&gt;fixed&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;10pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;10pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="table.data.caption" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-family"&gt;sans-serif&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;start&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;3pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after.precedence"&gt;2&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="keep-with-next.within-page"&gt;always&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="table.data.th" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="background-color"&gt;#DDDDDD&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-style"&gt;solid&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-width"&gt;1pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-start"&gt;0.3em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-end"&gt;0.2em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-before"&gt;2pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-after"&gt;2pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="table.data.td" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-style"&gt;solid&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-width"&gt;1pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-start"&gt;0.3em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-end"&gt;0.2em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-before"&gt;2pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="padding-after"&gt;2pt&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates that process the table</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="table"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table-and-caption &gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="title"&gt;
      &lt;fo:table-caption xsl:use-attribute-sets="table.data.caption"&gt;
        &lt;fo:block start-indent="0em"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="title" mode="make-title"/&gt;
       &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/fo:table-caption&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;fo:table xsl:use-attribute-sets="table.data"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:if test="@layout"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:attribute name="table-layout"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="@layout"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;xsl:if test="@width"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:attribute name="inline-progression-dimension"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="@width"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
    &lt;/fo:table&gt;
  &lt;/fo:table-and-caption&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="table/title"&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="col"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table-column column-number="{@number}" column-width="{@width}"/&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="thead"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table-header start-indent="0pt" end-indent="0pt" &gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:table-header&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="tfoot"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table-footer start-indent="0pt" end-indent="0pt" &gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:table-footer&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="tbody"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table-body start-indent="0pt" end-indent="0pt"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:table-body&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="tr"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:element name="fo:table-row"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="@height"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:attribute name="block-progression-dimension"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="@height"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="th"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table-cell xsl:use-attribute-sets="table.data.th"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:call-template name="cell-span"/&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="@valign"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="display-align"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="@valign"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;fo:block&gt;
      &lt;xsl:if test="@align"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="@align"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
    &lt;/fo:block&gt;
  &lt;/fo:table-cell&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="td"&gt;
  &lt;fo:table-cell xsl:use-attribute-sets="table.data.td"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:call-template name="cell-span"/&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="@valign"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="display-align"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="@valign"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;fo:block &gt;
      &lt;xsl:if test="@align"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="@align"/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
    &lt;/fo:block&gt;
  &lt;/fo:table-cell&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="cell-span"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:if test="@colspan"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:attribute name="number-columns-spanned"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="@colspan"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
  &lt;xsl:if test="@rowspan"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:attribute name="number-rows-spanned"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="@rowspan"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The stylesheet looks long, though, it is only to map the element name of the SimpleDoc to that of XSL formatting object. Below shows the points.
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The layout property defined for the table element is set for the layout property of fo:table to control the automatic table layout. The value of auto or fixed is valid.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The width attribute defined for the table element is set for <fo:inline id="ERBAG">inline-progression-dimension property</fo:inline> of fo:table object as the width of the entire table.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The number, width attributes defined for the col element is set for <fo:inline id="EVBAG">column-number</fo:inline>, <fo:inline id="EXBAG">column-width</fo:inline> property of the <fo:inline id="EZBAG">fo:table-column</fo:inline> object. Then, the column width can be specified. It's possible to specify the column width not by the fixed number but by % value. There are various ways to specify parameter, such as specifying an absolute value to the width attribute of the table element, or specifying the width of the table column as % value
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(9)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(9)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>Furthermore, there is a way to specify an absolute value for a part of the columns, specify <fo:inline id="E4BAG">proportional-column-width() function</fo:inline> to the rest of the columns and share width of the cells proportionally. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote>.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">4.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The height property defined for the tr element is set for block-progression-dimension of the fo:table-row object. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">5.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The colspan, rowspan properties defined for the th, td elements are set to each number-columns-spanned, number-rows-spanned of <fo:inline id="EGCAG">fo:table-cell</fo:inline> object. In addition, the align, valign propertieare set to <fo:inline id="EICAG">text-align property</fo:inline>, display-align property of fo:table-cell. In this way the text in the cell can be aligned.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block break-before="page" /><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ELCAG" axf:outline-level="2">Example of Table Construction</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Below is an example of table construction.</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">If nothing is specified, the table width will be divided by the number of columns and the width of the column will be given equally. </fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-number="1" column-width="33%" /><fo:table-column column-number="2" column-width="33%" /><fo:table-column column-number="3" column-width="33%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>
Symbol
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>
How to read
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block>

</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>,</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block> comma </fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>Means that elements appear in the same order in that element inside the document.

Means that only one element can be described.

</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">*</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">asterisk</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Means that the element appears zero or more times.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">+</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">plus</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Means that the element appears one or more time.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">( )</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">parentheses</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Means to group plural numbers of elements in the parentheses.</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block></fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em" display-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center">empty</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
Means that only one element can be described.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
When you specify the vertical alignment in the cell of the table, be sure of the following point. vertical-align can be specified in HTML, vertical-alignment can be specified in CSS2, however, the property which corresponds to this in XSL becomes <fo:inline id="EUGAG">display-align</fo:inline> instead of vertical-align. valign also maps to display-align in the stylesheet shown here. In XSL, vertical-align is applied only to the element of the inline level element.
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb1">16</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Processing List Elements</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EWGAG" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Processing List Elements</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In SimpleDoc, three list elements with which the format of the label portion of an item differs, a list with (1) number (ordered list), a (2) numbers-less list (unordered list), and (3) definition type list <fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(10)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(10)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block> definition type list is the itemized statements which specify a label character sequence for every item like a glossary. </fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote> (definition list) are defined.
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The list element (ol, ul, and dl) of SimpleDoc is constructed in the format with which the label  and the body part of the list are lined in horizontal mode.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
But, the definition type element (dl) also make it possible to format that the label and the body of the list are lined in vertical mode.
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(11)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(11)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>This is the same display format as the  browser format of dt in HTML.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote></fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>The ordered list element (ol) make it possible to take various types of numbers that are set in the labels.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The unordered list elements (ul) make it possible to specify various types of bullets that are set in the labels.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EIHAG" axf:outline-level="2">Comparing the List of SimpleDoc with the List of XSL</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In order to put the list elements to both the label of the list and body of the list, it is neccessary to transform them to fo:list-block in XSL. Let us compare lists of SimpleDoc with those of XSL formatting objects.</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="17.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="22.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="60%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Element </fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Meaning</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block text-align="center"> Definition</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>ol</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>ordered list</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(li)* </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>ul</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>unordered list</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(li)* </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>li</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>list item</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
(a group of inline elements)* </fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>dl</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>definition list</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(dt, dd)*</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>dt</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>definition term</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
(a group of inline elements)*</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>dd</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>definition details</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
(a group of inline elements)*
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">On the other hand, the list of XSL-FO has the following structure.
</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="17.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="22.5%" /><fo:table-column column-width="60%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row block-progression-dimension="1em"><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block> Element</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block> Meaning</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block> Definition</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>list-block</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
formatting object that formats lists
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(list-item+)<fo:block />provisional-distance-between-starts : Specify the distance between the start indent of the fo:list-item-label and the start indent of the fo:list-item-body.

<fo:block />
provisional-label-separation : Specify the  distance between the end of the list-item-label and the start of the list item body.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>list-item</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
list item including list label and list body.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(list-item-label,list-item-body)
</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>list-item-label</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>label of a list item.
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(%block;)+</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>list-item-body</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>
body of a list item
</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>(%block;)+</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Both correspondence relation is shown in a figure.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/list-struct_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">List of SimpleDoc and XSL</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The followings are remarkable differences between two.</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
As for ul and ol in HTML, the browser generates the label of a list automatically. In XSL-FO, you have to create it in a label region by using the stylesheet. For such occasions, the flexibility is high and the label format which is equal to the  practical use for publication can be made.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>As for dl, you should just arrange the contents of dt to a label region by using the stylesheet.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
There is no function to calculate the width of the fo:list-item-label formatting object in XSL-FO. An appropriate value must be specified in the  stylesheet.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Each template is explained below:</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EKKAG" axf:outline-level="2">Templates that Process the Ordered List</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">The ol templates for ordered list</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:param name="list-startdist-default" select="string('2em')"/&gt;
&lt;xsl:param name="list-gap-default" select="string('0.5em')"/&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="list.item" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;0.4em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;0.4em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="relative-align"&gt;baseline&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="ol"&gt;
  &lt;!-- determine the distance between the start  of the list-item-label and the start of the list-item-body, the distance between the end of the list-item-label and the start of the list-item-body. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="start-dist-local"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="./@startdist"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="./@startdist"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="$list-startdist-default"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;

  &lt;xsl:variable name="gap-local"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="./@gap"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="./@gap"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="$list-gap-default"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;


  &lt;!-- generate fo:list-block --&gt;
  &lt;fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="{$start-dist-local}"
                 provisional-label-separation="{$gap-local}" &gt;
    &lt;!-- Process the descendants of li --&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="ol/li"&gt;
  &lt;fo:list-item  xsl:use-attribute-sets="list.item"&gt;
    &lt;!-- generate list-item-label--&gt;
    &lt;!-- the end position of the list-item-label is calculated by
         label-end() function --&gt;
    &lt;!-- label format is specified in the type attribute.
         The initial value is '1'.--&gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="../@type"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:number format="{../@type}"/&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
            &lt;xsl:number format="1."/&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
       &lt;!-- generate the list-item-body --&gt;
    &lt;!-- The start position of the list-item-label is calculated by
         body-start() function --&gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"  text-align="justify" &gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;!-- the descendants of li are specified by the descendants of templates. --&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EPKAG" axf:outline-level="3">
Specifying the positions of label and body
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">When formatting a list, it is important to position the label and the body. In the fo:list-block:
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>provisional-distance-between-starts specifies the distance between the start of the list-item-label and the start of the list-item-body

</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>provisional-label-separation specifies the distance between the end of the list-item-label and the start of the list-item-body.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="inherit" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The template sets these values to the startdist, gap attributes of the ol element. But actually the list-item-label and list-item-body are specified as descendants of the fo:list-item. In order to specify the position of the end of the list-item-label and the start of the list-item-body, the label-end(), body-start() functions are used in the template.
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(12)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(12)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>These are called 'Property Value Function' in the XSL Specification.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote>
These two functions calculate the position by referring the values of provisional-distance-between-starts, provisional-distance-between-starts specified in fo:list-block.
<fo:footnote><fo:inline baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(13)</fo:inline><fo:footnote-body><fo:block font-size="0.9em" text-indent="0em" start-indent="0em" text-align="left"><fo:list-block provisional-label-separation="2pt" provisional-distance-between-starts="15pt"><fo:list-item><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block baseline-shift="super" font-size="75%">(13)</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>
label-end() =  (the content-width of fo:list-block) -  (provisional-distance-between-starts + start-indent of the label - provisional-label-separation)
<fo:block />
body-start() = (start-indent of the label) + (provisional-distance-between-starts)
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block></fo:footnote-body></fo:footnote></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">These function specification is just a manner. If you understand how to layout lists, it may be no problem to apply these mechanically.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E6KAG" axf:outline-level="3">Label Format</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The list label consists of a sequence of numbers. A sequence of numbers is generated by the default &lt;xsl:number format="1."/&gt;. <fo:inline id="EDLAG">xsl:number</fo:inline> counts the same level (sibling) of the li elements in the XML source document, returns a sequence number of the current li elements. Numbers are processed correctly even if the lists are nested.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ol-labelnumber_en.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Ordered list labels processed by xsl:number</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The label format is specified with the type property of the ol element. For example, the label (01), (02), (03)... will be generated if type="(01) is specified . The following formats can be used for a number portion.</fo:block><fo:table-and-caption space-after="1em" text-align="center"><fo:table table-layout="auto" space-before="10pt" space-after="10pt" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" text-align="left"><fo:table-column column-width="15%" /><fo:table-column column-width="40%" /><fo:table-header><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block> Form</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell background-color="#EEEEEE" border-style="solid" border-width="1pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-weight="bold" font-size="0.9em" text-align="center"><fo:block> Output</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-header><fo:table-body><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>a</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell
