ac...</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>A</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>A, B, C, D,...X, Y, Z, AA, AB, AC...</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>i</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>i, ii, iii, iv, v, vi, vii, viii, ix, x,...</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row><fo:table-row><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>I</fo:block></fo:table-cell><fo:table-cell border-style="solid" border-width="0.5pt" padding-start="0.3em" padding-end="0.2em" padding-before="2pt" padding-after="2pt" font-size="0.9em"><fo:block>I, II, III, IV, V, VI, VII, VIII, IX, X,...</fo:block></fo:table-cell></fo:table-row></fo:table-body></fo:table></fo:table-and-caption><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The type property specifies UNICODE characters that represent zero, 1 and punctuation marks such as parentheses. As the label formatcan be specified in the XML source document, the document can be made flexibly.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ELMAG" axf:outline-level="3">Example of Ordered List
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">XML source data</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;ol type="a."&gt;
  &lt;li&gt;type of list
    &lt;ol type="i)"&gt;
      &lt;li&gt;unordered list&lt;/li&gt;
      &lt;li&gt;ordered list&lt;/li&gt;
      &lt;li&gt;definition list&lt;/li&gt;
    &lt;/ol&gt;
  &lt;/li&gt;
  &lt;li&gt;list element
    &lt;ol&gt;
      &lt;li&gt;row&lt;/li&gt;
      &lt;li&gt;column&lt;/li&gt;
      &lt;li&gt;cell&lt;/li&gt;
    &lt;/ol&gt;
  &lt;/li&gt;
  &lt;li&gt;block element and inline element&lt;/li&gt;
&lt;/ol&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Following is the output result.
</fo:block><fo:block border="solid" border-width="thin" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">
&lt;fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;a.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt; type of list
&lt;fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;i)&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;unordered list&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;ii)&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;ordered list&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;iii)&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;definition list&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;b.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;list element&lt;fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;1.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;row&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;2.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;column&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;3.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;cell&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item relative-align="baseline"&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
&lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;c.&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;block element and inline element&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EVMAG" axf:outline-level="2">Templates that Process the Unordered List</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates for unordered list</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:param name="list-startdist-default" select="string('2em')"/&gt;
&lt;xsl:param name="list-gap-default" select="string('0.5em')"/&gt;
&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="list.item" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;0.4em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;0.4em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="relative-align"&gt;baseline&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="ul"&gt;
  &lt;!-- determine the distance between the start of the list-item-label and the start of the list-item-body, the distance between the end of the list-item-label and the start of the list-item-body. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="start-dist-local"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="./@startdist"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="./@startdist"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="$list-startdist-default"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;

  &lt;xsl:variable name="gap-local"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="./@gap"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="./@gap"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="$list-gap-default"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;

  &lt;!-- Generate fo:list-block. --&gt;
  &lt;fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="{$start-dist-local}"
                 provisional-label-separation="{$gap-local}" &gt;
    &lt;!-- Process the descendants of li --&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="ul/li"&gt;
  &lt;fo:list-item xsl:use-attribute-sets="list.item" &gt;
      &lt;!-- Generate list label.--&gt;
      &lt;!-- The end position of the label is calculated by label-end()function. --&gt;
      &lt;!-- The characters for label of line are specified in the type attribute.
           Initial value is “&amp;#x2022;” --&gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="../@type='disc'"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:text&gt;●&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="../@type='circle'"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:text&gt;○&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="../@type='square'"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:text&gt;□&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:when test="../@type='bsquare'"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:text&gt;■&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
          &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
            &lt;xsl:text&gt;&amp;#x2022;&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
    &lt;!-- Generate the list body.--&gt;
    &lt;!-- The starting position of the label is calculated by
         the body-start() function --&gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify" &gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E1MAG" axf:outline-level="3">Specify characters for label of line</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The difference between the ol and ul templates is only label processing. In the case of unordered list, the characters are set in the label. Types of characters can be specified in the type property in the ul element.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Next template is an example of the template that place an image as a character for label of line. Specify the image file by img:file name in the type property defined for the ul element.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Template that use an image as a character for label of line</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!-- The template that use an image as a character for label of line.--&gt;
&lt;xsl:template match="ul[substring(@type,1,4)='img:']/li"&gt;
  &lt;fo:list-item  xsl:use-attribute-sets="list.item" &gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block text-align="end"&gt;
        &lt;fo:external-graphic src="{substring-after(../@type,substring(../@type,1,4))}"
         content-height="1.2em" content-width="1.2em"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify" &gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EBNAG" axf:outline-level="3">
An example of unordered list
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">

&lt;fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"&gt;

&lt;fo:external-graphic src="img/bullet-star.png" content-height="12pt" content-width="12pt"/&gt;
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;

&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
&lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"&gt;
&lt;fo:block&gt;
block element and inline element
&lt;/fo:block&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ERNAG" axf:outline-level="2">
Templates that Process the Definition List
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The following problem occurs when transforming the definition list into fo:list-block formatting object.
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>In the SimpleDoc specification, child of dl element is supposed to appear in dt, dd order (dt,dd)*, but in HTML the condition is more relaxed. The pattern of only dt, only dd also exist.

<fo:inline font-weight="bold">&lt;!ELEMENT DL (DT|DD)+ &gt;</fo:inline></fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block><fo:inline id="EZNAG">dt</fo:inline> can be mapped to <fo:inline id="E2NAG">fo:list-item-label</fo:inline>, <fo:inline id="E4NAG">dd</fo:inline> can be mapped to <fo:inline id="E6NAG">fo:list-item-body</fo:inline>. But there are no tags to be mapped to generate fo:list-item in the XML source document.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
It is better to be able to process definition list like HTML also in XSL. But the above two problem cannot be solved by the data driven stylesheet which process the tags in the XML source document in appearing order. It is necessary to find a pair of dt, dd in the XML source document. Following is the template that realize this process. The template is a remodel of the sample XSL stylesheest described in the XSL specification.
</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ECOAG" axf:outline-level="3">Templates of definition list
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Templates of definition list</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="dt" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="font-weight"&gt;bold&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="dd.list" &gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-before"&gt;0.3em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="space-after"&gt;0.5em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;justify&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:attribute-set name="dd.block" use-attribute-sets="dd.list"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="start-indent" &gt;from-parent() + 4em&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
  &lt;xsl:attribute name="text-align"&gt;justify&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
&lt;/xsl:attribute-set&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="dl"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="@type='list'"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:call-template name="dl.format.list"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
      &lt;xsl:call-template name="dl.format.block"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="dl.format.block"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="dl.format.list"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="start-dist-local"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="./@startdist"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="./@startdist"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="$dl-startdist-default"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;

  &lt;xsl:variable name="gap-local"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="./@gap"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="./@gap"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="$dl-gap-default"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;

  &lt;fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="{$start-dist-local}"
                 provisional-label-separation="{$gap-local}" &gt;
    &lt;xsl:call-template name="process.dl.list"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template name="process.dl.list"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:param name="dts" select="/.."/&gt;
  &lt;xsl:param name="dds" select="/.."/&gt;
  &lt;xsl:param name="nodes" select="*"/&gt;

  &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="count($nodes)=0"&gt;
      &lt;!-- data end : Process the elements stocked in dts, dds. --&gt;
      &lt;xsl:if test="count($dts)&gt;0 or count($dds)&gt;0"&gt;
        &lt;fo:list-item  xsl:use-attribute-sets="list.item"&gt;
          &lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="$dts"/&gt;
          &lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
          &lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="$dds"/&gt;
          &lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
        &lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;

    &lt;xsl:when test="name($nodes[1])='dd'"&gt;
      &lt;!-- dd is stored in dds fnction, call itself recursively.--&gt;
      &lt;xsl:call-template name="process.dl.list"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:with-param name="dts" select="$dts"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:with-param name="dds" select="$dds|$nodes[1]"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:with-param name="nodes" select="$nodes[position()&gt;1]"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:call-template&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;

    &lt;xsl:when test="name($nodes[1])='dt'"&gt;
      &lt;!-- Process the elements stocked in dts, dds. --&gt;
      &lt;xsl:if test="count($dts)&gt;0 or count($dds)&gt;0"&gt;
        &lt;fo:list-item  xsl:use-attribute-sets="list.item"&gt;
          &lt;fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="$dts"/&gt;
          &lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
          &lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"&gt;
            &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="$dds"/&gt;
          &lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
        &lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;!-- dt is stored in dts variable, call itself recursively.--&gt;
      &lt;xsl:call-template name="process.dl.list"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:with-param name="dts" select="$nodes[1]"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:with-param name="nodes" select="$nodes[position()&gt;1]"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:call-template&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;

    &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
      &lt;!-- The children of dl must be only dt, dd. --&gt;
      &lt;!-- Unfortunately, xsl:message does not work in MSXML3. --&gt;
      &lt;xsl:message&gt;
        &lt;xsl:text&gt;
         (The elements except dt,dd are specified as a child of dl element.
        &lt;/xsl:text&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="name($nodes[1])"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:text&gt;).&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:message&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="dt"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:element name="fo:block" use-attribute-sets="dt"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="../@mode='debug'"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-color"&gt;blue&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-style"&gt;dashed&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-width" &gt;thin&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="dd"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
    &lt;xsl:when test="../@type='list'"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:element name="fo:block" use-attribute-sets="dd.list"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:if test="../@mode='debug'"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-color"&gt;red&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-style"&gt;solid&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-width" &gt;thin&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
    &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
      &lt;xsl:element name="fo:block" use-attribute-sets="dd.block"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:if test="../@mode='debug'"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-color"&gt;red&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-style"&gt;solid&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
          &lt;xsl:attribute name="border-width" &gt;thin&lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:element&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In this stylesheet, you have to determine which transformation to use from the following type by the type attribute defined for the dl element:
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
list type as fo:list-block: the label (dt) and the body(dd) are lined in horizontal way.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>HTML type: the label (dt) and the body (dd) are lined in vertical way.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block><fo:block text-indent="inherit" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">When "list" is specified in the type attribute, select the first one.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In case of the list type, after generating fo:list-block, the process.dl.list template will process these. The process.dl.list template processes the following:
</fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">1.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The process.dl.list template take descendant elements of dl, start processing from the first element.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">2.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
After getting dt, dd, store each of them to the dts, dds variable in appearing order.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">3.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
When getting the next dt, take out dt, dd that are stored to dts, dls. Output fo:list-item and its descendants. Initialize the dts, dds, and store the dt to dts variable.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">4.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>
The above two processes are repeated until all the dt, dd are taken out.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">5.</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>It is the end of the process when all the dt, dd under dl, are processed. If there are still dt, dd left in the dts, dds variable, take out these and output fo:list-item and its descendants.
</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="13pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="14pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EUOAG" axf:outline-level="3">Example of a definition list
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The following is a sample XML source data of definition list.
</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">A sample data of the definition list</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;dl&gt;
  &lt;dt&gt;Type of lists&lt;/dt&gt;
    &lt;dd&gt;There are three kinds of lists, that is unordered list, ordered list, and definition list.
    &lt;dl class="list"&gt;
      &lt;dt&gt;From here&lt;/dt&gt;
      &lt;dd&gt;These are nested lists&lt;/dd&gt;
      &lt;dd&gt;The dd that does not match dt.&lt;/dd&gt;
      &lt;dt&gt;The dt without the dd&lt;/dt&gt;
      &lt;dt&gt;unordered list&lt;/dt&gt;
      &lt;dd&gt;Unordered lists are classified as square, circle and so on, according to the characters for label of line.&lt;/dd&gt;
      &lt;dt&gt;Ordered lists&lt;/dt&gt;
      &lt;dd&gt;Ordered lists have various kinds of types according to the label format.&lt;/dd&gt;
    &lt;/dl&gt;
  &lt;/dd&gt;
  &lt;dt&gt;The elements that construct the table&lt;/dt&gt;
  &lt;dd&gt;fo:The table consists of table-caption, fo-table-caption, fo:table, fo:table-column, fo:table-head, fo:table-foot, fo:table-body, fo:table-row, fo:table-cell&lt;/dd&gt;
  &lt;dt&gt;kinds of color&lt;/dt&gt;
  &lt;dd&gt;16 kinds of colors can be used, such as red, blue, white, black and so on. Also it is possible to specify colors by RGB() functions.&lt;/dd&gt;
&lt;/dl&gt;</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The following figure shows how fo:list-item is generated from the dt, dl. fo-list-item #1-n is generated from the first dl. #2-n is generated from the nested dl.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/deflist-procen.emf"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Transforming the definition list into the list type.

</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The process.dl.list template calls itself recursively. In the general programming language, it is natural to assign a value to a variable and  process using a variable. But in XSL, it is impossible to assign a value to a variable, but it is possible to initialize a value instead. Loops are formed by taking recursive process.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
For HTML type, the dl.format.block template transforms. Only the template have to do is to call the descendant templates in order to process dt, dd in appearing order.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The following is the output of list type transformation. To make it look better, fo:list-item-label and fo:list-item-body are bordered.

</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb2">17</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Functions for creating PDF</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="ELPAG" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Functions for creating PDF</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">With XSL Formatter, the following relates with PDF generation are available.</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Set the document information in the result <fo:inline id="EVPAG">PDF</fo:inline>.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Create bookmars in the result PDF.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Set up the <fo:inline id="E1PAG">link </fo:inline>to a PDF document (from a table of contents to the body text, for example).</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Set up the link to the <fo:inline id="E5PAG">external destination </fo:inline>.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Although some of the functions described here in creating PDF are not defined in the specification of XSL-FO V1.0, it's possible by using <fo:inline id="ECQAG">Antenna House extension specification</fo:inline><fo:basic-link internal-destination="a4"><fo:inline>(Source Information
 [4])</fo:inline></fo:basic-link>.</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EGQAG" axf:outline-level="2">PDF document information</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Although the document information cannot be set up by XSL-FO V1.0 specification in case a formatted result is outputted to PDF, it's possible to set up the document information by Antenna House extension specification. The definition is given using <fo:inline id="EKQAG">axf:document-info</fo:inline>. If axf:document-info is directly under <fo:inline id="EMQAG">fo:root</fo:inline>, and it exists before <fo:inline id="EOQAG">fo:page-sequence</fo:inline> appears, it will be reflected. In the style sheet, title, subtitle, and author are set up from "/doc/head" of the <fo:inline id="EQQAG">SimpleDoc</fo:inline> as PDF document information as follows.</fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" font-weight="bold" keep-with-next.within-page="always" space-before="1em" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em">Outputting PDF document information</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="doc"&gt;
  &lt;fo:root xmlns:fo="http://www.w3.org/1999/XSL/Format"&gt;
    &lt;axf:document-info name="title" value="{/doc/head/title}"/&gt;
    &lt;axf:document-info name="subject" value="{/doc/head/subtitle}"/&gt;
    &lt;axf:document-info name="author" value="{/doc/head/author}"/&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EVQAG" axf:outline-level="2">Creating a <fo:inline id="EYQAG">bookmark</fo:inline></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">PDF bookmarks use <fo:inline id="E2QAG">Antenna House extension specification</fo:inline><fo:basic-link internal-destination="a4"><fo:inline>(Source Information
 [4])</fo:inline></fo:basic-link> similarly. In this case, it becomes possible by specifying <fo:inline id="E6QAG">axf:outline-level</fo:inline> and <fo:inline id="EBRAG">axf:outline-title</fo:inline> to be <fo:inline id="EDRAG">fo:block</fo:inline> to output to a bookmark. When there is no axf:outline-title, the contents of fo:block serves as a bookmark automatically. When processing the title of part | chapter | section | subsection | subsubsection | appendix, axf:outline-level is set up and the bookmark is made to output in SD2FO-DOC.xsl. The template is &lt;xsl:template name="title.out"&gt; (sub template for outputting a title).</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template name="title.out"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="level" select="count(ancestor-or-self::part | ancestor-or-self::chapter |
     ancestor-or-self::section | ancestor-or-self::subsection |ancestor-or-self::subsubsection
     |ancestor-or-self::appendix )"/&gt;
    &lt;xsl:choose&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="$level=1"&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h1" id="{generate-id()}" axf:outline-level="{$level}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="$level=2"&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h2" id="{generate-id()}" axf:outline-level="{$level}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="$level=3"&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h3" id="{generate-id()}" axf:outline-level="{$level}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="$level=4"&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h4" id="{generate-id()}" axf:outline-level="{$level}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:when test="$level=5"&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h5" id="{generate-id()}" axf:outline-level="{$level}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:when&gt;
      &lt;xsl:otherwise&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="h5" id="{generate-id()}"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="title.out.sub"/&gt;
          &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:otherwise&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:choose&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EGRAG" axf:outline-level="2">Link setting</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always"><fo:inline id="EJRAG">fo:basic-link</fo:inline> is used to<fo:inline id="a-link"> setup <fo:inline id="EORAG">links</fo:inline></fo:inline>.  The reference destination id is specified using the internal-destination property to create a link into the same document. At this time, the XSL-FO object of the reference origin needs to have the id of the same value. In case of external links, the reference destination is specified with the external-destination property. In SimpleDoc, both internal/external links are expressed using the a element. The reference destination is specified by the href property and when the reference destination starts with "#", an internal link is set up, otherwise an external link is set up. </fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="a[@href]"&gt;
  &lt;fo:basic-link&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="starts-with(@href,'#')"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="internal-destination"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="substring-after(@href,'#')"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;fo:inline xsl:use-attribute-sets="a"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
    &lt;xsl:if test="starts-with(@href,'#')=false"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:attribute name="external-destination"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="@href"/&gt;
      &lt;/xsl:attribute&gt;
      &lt;fo:inline xsl:use-attribute-sets="a"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:variable name="anchor-texts"&gt;
          &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;
        &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:if test="@href!=$anchor-texts"&gt;
          &lt;fo:inline&gt;
            &lt;xsl:text&gt;(&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
            &lt;xsl:value-of select="@href"/&gt;
            &lt;xsl:text&gt;)&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
          &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
  &lt;/fo:basic-link&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The element with the name element as a reference destination is processed as an inline object which has id as follows.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="a[@name]"&gt;
  &lt;fo:inline id="{@name}"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Moreover, it is also possible to set a link to the portion where it corresponds in a document from a table of contents or an index. In this case, id used for reference creates id automatically using the generate-id() function.  When the generate-id() function is called, XSLT processor will create a suitable character sequence like "IDXP83DL" corresponding to a current node for id.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In the case of a table of contents, the portion which outputs an item by the toc.line template is described as follows.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">
&lt;fo:basic-link internal-destination="{generate-id()}"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:value-of select="title"/&gt;
&lt;/fo:basic-link&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Set id using generate-id() also when outputting a title in the text used as the reference destination. The value of id generated by the generate-id() function is always the same among the same elements, and surely different against different elements.</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb3">18</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Reference to Appendix</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EXRAG" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Reference to Appendix</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Put data numbers automatically to the appendix list at the end of the book.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Create the corresponding data numbers automatically for the reference to the reference data in the text.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Create an appendix list in the end of the book, and make it possible to refer to the appendix at the end of the book by the data numbers in the text. Even if it generates these data numbers automatically and revises the appendix list, it is made not to need to update the reference numbers in the text while editing.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The whole appendix list is expressed with the <fo:inline id="EFSAG">bib element</fo:inline>, and each data is made into the contents of the li element in <fo:inline id="EHSAG">SimpleDoc.dtd</fo:inline>. The ID number is given to the li element. Data numbers are automatically put at the appendix list. The stylesheet for this is as follows.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="bib"&gt;
  &lt;fo:list-block&gt;
    &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="li"/&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-block&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;

&lt;xsl:template match="bib/li"&gt;
  &lt;fo:list-item end-indent="label-end()" id="{@id}"&gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-label&gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;xsl:text&gt;[&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="position()"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:text&gt;]&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-label&gt;
    &lt;fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="."/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:list-item-body&gt;
  &lt;/fo:list-item&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The appendix is referred by the ref element, ref-id="<fo:inline font-style="italic">xxx </fo:inline>"in the text. (<fo:inline font-style="italic">xxx </fo:inline> is the id value of the li element of the reference destination.) The stylesheet which generates this reference label is as follows.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template match="ref"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="target"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:call-template name="get-position"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:with-param name="id-value" select="@ref-id"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:call-template&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:variable&gt;
  &lt;fo:basic-link internal-destination="{@ref-id}"&gt;
    &lt;fo:inline&gt;
      &lt;xsl:text&gt;（Source Information [&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="$target"/&gt;
      &lt;xsl:text&gt;]）&lt;/xsl:text&gt;
    &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
  &lt;/fo:basic-link&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Since the reference destination of the ref element shows the turn of the li element in the bib element, then the position() function calculates what number the li element comes whose value of ref-id matches in the bib element.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb4">19</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Index</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="ESSAG" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Index</fo:block><fo:block space-before="1em" space-after="1em" border-style="solid" border-color="gray" border-width="1.5pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em"><fo:block font-weight="bold" text-decoration="underline" space-after="0.5em" font-size="0.8em" keep-with-next.within-page="always"></fo:block><fo:list-block provisional-distance-between-starts="2em" provisional-label-separation="0.5em"><fo:list-item space-before="0.4em" space-after="0.4em" relative-align="baseline"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block text-align="end">・</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()" text-align="justify"><fo:block>Create indexes at the end of the book.</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Here in this section, the creation method of an index is explained sequentially. The templates for indexes are put together in index.xsl. For more details, see also the contents of index.xsl.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The index element is defined by SimpleDoc for the items put on an index.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:key name="index-key" match="index" use="substring(@key,1,1)"/&gt;
  &lt;xsl:key name="index-value" match="index" use="."/&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="E4SAG" axf:outline-level="2">Creating keys</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Declare the key with a name using xsl:key in order to group the index elements by using the beginning of the character.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:key name="index-key" match="index" use="substring(@key,1,1)"/&gt;
  &lt;xsl:key name="index-value" match="index" use="."/&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Since <fo:inline id="EDTAG">xsl:key</fo:inline> must be a top-level element within a stylesheet, it is described at the head of the SD2FO-DOC.xsl stylesheet. The first xsl:key declares the head-one character of the key property to the key named index-key as a value. Like an English document, if it's possible to group the index elements by their contents, it's accomplished by the method using use="substring(1 ., 1) ", without using the key property. For the second xsl:key, the content of the index element is declared as a value to the key named index-value. This is used to sort and output keys in the grouped node set with the head-one character.
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EFTAG" axf:outline-level="2">Creating an index page</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Creation of an index is started from the index.create template in the index.xsl stylesheet. Like other pages, <fo:inline id="EJTAG">fo:page-sequence</fo:inline> and <fo:inline id="ELTAG">fo:flow</fo:inline> are generated in the beginning, and next, a title is outputted at the head of the index page.</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
Next, the index elements for numbers and alphabets are processed.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template name="index.create"&gt;
  &lt;fo:page-sequence master-reference="PageMaster-index"&gt;
    &lt;!-- Set a document name in the header region. --&gt;
    &lt;fo:static-content flow-name="xsl-region-before"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block font-size="7pt" text-align="center" border-after-width="thin" border-after-style="solid"&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="/doc/head/title"/&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:static-content&gt;
    &lt;fo:flow flow-name="xsl-region-body"&gt;
      &lt;fo:block&gt;
        &lt;!-- The title is spaned all.--&gt;
        &lt;fo:block span="all" line-height="15mm" background-color="#9bd49d" text-align="center" font-size="20pt" space-after="10mm" axf:outline-level="1" id="index-page"&gt;
          INDEX
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
        &lt;fo:block span="all"&gt;
          &amp;#xA0;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
        &lt;fo:block xsl:use-attribute-sets="index"&gt;
          &lt;!-- Numbers and alphabets. --&gt;
          &lt;xsl:call-template name="index.create.mainALPHA"/&gt;
          &lt;xsl:if test="(/doc/@lang = 'ja') or (/doc/@lang = '') or not(/doc/@lang)"&gt;
            &lt;!-- Japanese Kana --&gt;
            &lt;xsl:call-template name="index.create.mainKANA"/&gt;
          &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
        &lt;/fo:block&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/fo:flow&gt;
  &lt;/fo:page-sequence&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EPTAG" axf:outline-level="2">Grouping and taking out the index elements</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">"index.create.mainALPHA" is the template which generates the index of alphabets. The following shows the examle using "index.create.mainALPHA" </fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">What is considered to be difficult in creating an index is to group the target nodes and take them out. In order to group them, xsl:key which is mentioned above and the data in the head of index.xsl are used.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;!DOCTYPE DOCUMENT [
&lt;!ENTITY ALPHA "'@1234567890ABCDEFGHIJKLMNOPQRSTUVWXYZ'"&gt;
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Each alphabet character is defined as an entity and it is used for grouping. Characters are taken out one by one from the entity, and then the node set which has the character as a key is taken out.
</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template name="index.create.mainALPHA"&gt;
  &lt;xsl:param name="lettersALPHA" select="&amp;ALPHA;"/&gt;
  &lt;!-- (1) Process any one from 0 to 9, or from A to Z. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:call-template name="index.create.section"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:with-param name="letter" select="substring($lettersALPHA,1,1)"/&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:call-template&gt;
  &lt;!-- (2) Prepare for processing the following one from 0 to 9, or from A to Z. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="remainderALPHA" select="substring($lettersALPHA,2)"/&gt;
  &lt;!-- (3) process the following one from 0 to 9, or from A to Z. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:if test="$remainderALPHA"&gt;
    &lt;xsl:call-template name="index.create.mainALPHA"&gt;
      &lt;xsl:with-param name="lettersALPHA" select="$remainderALPHA"/&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:call-template&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">In the portion (1), one character used as a key is passed to the "index.create.section" template as a parameter, and a node set is processed in the "index.create.section" template. In (2), the following one character is taken out and all characters are processed by calling  "$remainderALPHA" recursively by (3).
</fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EXTAG" axf:outline-level="2">Node set output</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The "index.create.section" template outputs a node set which has a character used as index-key.</fo:block><fo:block white-space="pre" wrap-option="wrap" background-color="#EEEEEE" font-family="monospace" font-size="9pt" padding="0.5em" start-indent="0.5em" end-indent="0.5em">&lt;xsl:template name="index.create.section"&gt;
    &lt;!--  Receive the character to be processed. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:param name="letter"/&gt;
  &lt;!-- Set the nodes who have the 'letter' value of the key to the terms variable and sort them.--&gt;
  &lt;xsl:variable name="terms" select="key('index-key',$letter)"/&gt;
  &lt;!-- Get the index which has the same head-one character
       as the parameter which received. --&gt;
  &lt;xsl:if test="$terms"&gt;
    &lt;!-- Output key characters. --&gt;
    &lt;fo:block font-weight="bold" text-align="center" space-before="1em"&gt;
      &lt;!-- Output the received one character as is. --&gt;
      &lt;xsl:value-of select="$letter"/&gt;
    &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;!-- Make it a rule not to process the same text redundantly. --&gt;
    &lt;xsl:for-each select="$terms[not(.=preceding::index)]"&gt;
      &lt;!-- Sort the text in key order. --&gt;
      &lt;xsl:sort select="@key"/&gt;
      &lt;fo:block text-align-last="justify" axf:suppress-duplicate-page-number="true"&gt;
        &lt;!-- Output the text as is. --&gt;
        &lt;xsl:value-of select="."/&gt;
        &lt;fo:leader leader-pattern="dots" leader-length.optimum="3em"/&gt;
        &lt;!-- Get the same text. --&gt;
        &lt;xsl:variable name="terms2" select="key('index-value',.)"/&gt;
        &lt;xsl:if test="$terms2"&gt;
          &lt;fo:inline&gt;
            &lt;!-- Output all of those page numbers when the same text exists
                 in two or more places. --&gt;
            &lt;xsl:apply-templates select="$terms2" mode="line"/&gt;
          &lt;/fo:inline&gt;
        &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
      &lt;/fo:block&gt;
    &lt;/xsl:for-each&gt;
  &lt;/xsl:if&gt;
&lt;/xsl:template&gt;</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">By using the <fo:inline id="E4TAG">axf:suppress-duplicate-page-number</fo:inline> property (<fo:inline id="E6TAG">Antenna House extension specification</fo:inline><fo:basic-link internal-destination="a4"><fo:inline>(Source Information
 [4])</fo:inline></fo:basic-link>), It is possible to suppress the duplicate page numbers.
</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/idx-d.svg"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Example result without using the axf:suppress-duplicate-page-number property</fo:block><fo:block text-align="center"><fo:external-graphic src="img/idx-nd.svg"></fo:external-graphic></fo:block><fo:block font-family="sans-serif" text-align="center" space-before="0.5em" space-after="1em" font-weight="bold" keep-with-previous.within-page="always" font-size="0.8em">Example result using the axf:suppress-duplicate-page-number property</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:marker marker-class-name="thumb5">20</fo:marker><fo:marker marker-class-name="section-title">Miscellaneous</fo:marker><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="ELUAG" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Miscellaneous</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EOUAG" axf:outline-level="2">Using modes</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">
The <fo:inline id="ESUAG">SD2FO-DOC.xsl stylesheet</fo:inline> includes the stylesheet called article.xsl. This stylesheet processes to format a document without a cover / table of contents / index, when class="article" is specified in the doc element of an XML document. mode is specified in all the templates as mode="article" and the processing is different from the template of the SD2FO-DOC.xsl stylesheet.  Thus, the processing of arbitrary elements can be divided by using the mode attribute for the template.
</fo:block></fo:block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="22pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-after="14pt" break-before="page" keep-with-next.within-page="always" border-after-style="solid" border-after-width="2pt" id="EUUAG" axf:outline-level="1"><fo:inline space-end="5pt"><fo:external-graphic src="img/ico4.png"></fo:external-graphic></fo:inline>Appendix</fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="EXUAG" axf:outline-level="2">Source Information
</fo:block><fo:list-block><fo:list-item id="a1" space-after="0.5em"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block>[1]</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>Extensible Stylesheet Language (XSL) Version 1.0, <fo:block />W3C Recommendation 15 October 2001, <fo:block /> http://www.w3.org/TR/2001/REC-xsl-20011015/</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item id="a2" space-after="0.5em"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block>[2]</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>XSL Transformations (XSLT) Version 1.0 <fo:block />W3C Recommendation 16 November 1999, <fo:block />http://www.w3.org/TR/xslt</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item id="a3" space-after="0.5em"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block>[3]</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>PureSmartDoc<fo:block />http://www.asahi-net.or.jp/~dp8t-asm/java/tools/</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item><fo:list-item id="a4" space-after="0.5em"><fo:list-item-label end-indent="label-end()"><fo:block>[4]</fo:block></fo:list-item-label><fo:list-item-body start-indent="body-start()"><fo:block>Antenna House Extension Specification<fo:block />http://www.antennahouse.com/xslfo/axf4-extension.htm</fo:block></fo:list-item-body></fo:list-item></fo:list-block></fo:block><fo:block><fo:block font-size="16pt" font-family="Arial" font-weight="bold" space-before="19pt" space-after="5pt" keep-with-next.within-page="always" id="ESVAG" axf:outline-level="2">Update History</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The original version of this tutorial was written in Japanese for XSL School, June 2001, Tokyo.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The English version of the tutorial was first released on October 23, 2001. It was based on Candidate Recommendation of XSL Specification.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Minor revised version was released on May 6th, 2002 in order to be conformant to Recommendation of XSL Specification Version 1.0.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">The 2nd Edition, released on February, 2005, was made by adding the contents of indexes, functions for PDF creation, reference to appendix and much more substantial contents.
</fo:block><fo:block text-indent="1em" space-before="0.6em" space-after="0.6em" text-align="justify" keep-together.within-page="always">Minor revised version was released on February,
